I have been working on updating and debugging a SOC Separation Script written in Python, which automates access removal for departing users at Marchex. The script interacts with LDAP, Request Tracker (RT), and various system APIs.

So far, we have:

Updated the script from Python 2 to Python 3

Converted rt_marchex.py and utils.py to be Python 3-compatible.
Replaced urllib2 with requests and updated print statements.
Resolved Python module import issues

Installed missing dependencies (ldap3, requests, openpyxl).
Fixed import paths for utils.py and rt_marchex.py.
Resolved errors related to missing rt and ldap3 functions.
Fixed LDAP connection problems

Addressed "AttributeError: module 'ldap3' has no attribute 'set_option'" by configuring TLS properly.
Replaced deprecated LDAP connection settings with Tls(validate=ssl.CERT_NONE).
Fixed "invalid server address" by defining LDAP_HOST and LDAP_PORT explicitly.
Implemented error handling for LDAP authentication failures (LDAPBindError).
Checked LDAP server connectivity

Ping to ldap.sea.marchex.com failed → Possible DNS or network misconfiguration.
Telnet to ldap.sea.marchex.com:636 failed → Possible firewall or LDAP service issue.
Adjusted LDAP connection settings to use use_ssl=True.
Improved error handling and logging

Added better logging for LDAP failures.
Handled LDAPBindError more gracefully.
Ensured missing system scripts (MISSING_SCRIPTS) are logged properly.
I need to continue debugging LDAP connectivity issues and verify access removal functions. In the next steps, I want to:

Ensure that the LDAP connection works as expected.
Verify that the separation script processes users correctly.
Fix any remaining issues with RT ticket queries and system access removals.
Let's continue troubleshooting from here! 🚀

import logging
import getpass
import ldap3 as ldap
import sys
import os
import ssl
import requests
import openpyxl
import json

sys.path.append(os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/lib/python"))

import utils 
import rt_marchex as rt
from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor
from ldap3 import Server, Connection, Tls, ALL
from ldap3.core.exceptions import LDAPBindError


# Setup logging     
logging.basicConfig(
    format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s',
    level=logging.INFO
)

# 🟢 Mock Mode (Secret Backdoor Enabled)
MOCK_MODE = False  # Default is OFF

# 🔐 Secret Backdoor Command (Toggle Mock Mode)
secret_command = getpass.getpass("Enter command or press Enter to continue: ").strip().lower()
if secret_command == "testmode":
    MOCK_MODE = True
    logging.warning("🚀 Test Mode Activated: Mock Mode is ENABLED.")
else:
    logging.info("Running in LIVE Mode.")

# Systems that require separation processing
SYSTEMS_CATALOG = {
    "AdTrack": True,
    "AFR": True,
    "Auth0": True,
    "Avenger": True,
    "AWS": True,
    "ADO": True,
    "AzurePortal": True,
    "CallScoring": True,
    "Chef": True,
    "Cuttlefish": True,
    "EmailAccess": True,
    "Engage": True,
    "EquityEdge_GreatPlains": True,
    "GitHub": True,
    "Grafana": True,
    "Ipplan": True,
    "JIRA": True,
    "Marchex.io": True,
    "MI5": True,
    "Microsites": True,
    "NewRelic": True,
    "Nexus": True,
    "NimUI": True,
    "NISMaps": True,
    "OpenVPN": True,
    "PagerDuty": True,
    "Pulley": True,
    "Postman": True,
    "RT": True, # Checking RT for past access requests
    "Slack": True,
    "MarketingEdge": True,
    "Sendgrid": True,
    "Sentry": True,
    "Snowflake": True,
    "TACACS": True,  # Needs special handling (SEV5 ticket)
    "Wallace": True,
    "XMSHammer": True
}

ACCESS_LIST = [system for system, enabled in SYSTEMS_CATALOG.items() if enabled]
MISSING_SCRIPTS = []

# LDAP Configurations
LDAP_HOST = 'ldap.sea.marchex.com'
LDAP_PORT = 636
LDAP_BASEDN = 'ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com'
LDAP_BINDDN = 'uid={user},ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com'
LDAP_SF = '(cn={user})'

# RT (Request Tracker) Configuration
RT_HOST = 'https://rt.marchex.com'
RT_URL = 'https://rt.marchex.com/REST/1.0'
RT_USER = "socbot"  # Replace with actual RT user
RT_PASS = "securepass"  # Replace with actual RT password

# High Priority Contact List Location
HIGH_PRI_FILE = r'\\marchex\files\soc\Emergency\High Priority Contact List\NOCHighPriorityContactList1.xlsx'


try:
    server = Server(LDAP_HOST, port=LDAP_PORT, use_ssl=True)
    logging.info(f"✅ Successfully connected to LDAP server: {LDAP_HOST}:{LDAP_PORT}")
except Exception as e:
    logging.error(f"❌ Failed to connect to LDAP server: {e}")
    sys.exit(1)


def get_user_input(prompt):
    """Wrapper for input to handle common input scenarios."""
    try:
        return input(prompt).strip()
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error getting user input: {e}")
        return None


def get_directory_info(user):
    """Query Directory Manager for user alias & manager name."""
    directory_url = f"https://directorymanager.marchex.com/api/user/{user}"
    try:
        response = requests.get(directory_url)
        response.raise_for_status()
        user_data = response.json()
        return user_data.get('alias', 'Unknown'), user_data.get('manager', 'Unknown')
    except Exception as e:
        logging.warning(f"Failed to retrieve Directory Manager info for {user}: {e}")
        return 'Unknown', 'Unknown'


def check_rt_for_access_tickets(user):
    """Check RT (Request Tracker) for past access requests related to this user."""
    logging.info(f"Checking RT for past access requests related to {user}...")
    query = f"Owner = '{user}' AND (Status = 'new' OR Status = 'open')"
    tracker = rt.Rt(RT_URL, RT_USER, RT_PASS)
    if not tracker.login():
        logging.error("Failed to authenticate with RT.")
        return
    try:
        tickets = tracker.search(Queue="SOC", raw_query=query)
        if tickets:
            logging.info(f"User {user} has {len(tickets)} past access tickets in RT.")
            for ticket in tickets:
                logging.info(f"RT Ticket Found: {ticket['id']} - {ticket['Subject']}")
        else:
            logging.info(f"No previous access tickets found in RT for {user}.")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.warning(f"Error checking RT for {user}: {e}")


def check_high_priority_contact_list(user):
    """Check and remove user from High Priority Contact List."""
    if not os.path.exists(HIGH_PRI_FILE):
        logging.warning("High Priority Contact List file not found.")
        return
    try:
        wb = openpyxl.load_workbook(HIGH_PRI_FILE)
        sheet = wb.active
        for row in sheet.iter_rows():
            for cell in row:
                if str(user).lower() in str(cell.value).lower():
                    logging.info(f"Removing {user} from High Priority Contact List.")
                    cell.value = None
                    wb.save(HIGH_PRI_FILE)
                    return
        logging.info(f"{user} not found in High Priority Contact List.")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error modifying High Priority Contact List: {e}")


def submit_sev5_ticket_for_TACACS(user):
    """Submit a SEV5 ticket to NetEng for TACACS removal."""
    logging.info(f"Submitting SEV5 ticket for TACACS removal for {user}.")
    
    # Simulated API request
    ticket_payload = {
        "summary": f"SEV5 - Remove TACACS access for {user}",
        "description": f"User {user} requires TACACS access removal as part of separation.",
        "priority": "SEV5",
        "assigned_team": "NetEng"
    }
    try:
        response = requests.post("https://ticketing.marchex.com/api/tickets", json=ticket_payload)
        response.raise_for_status()
        logging.info(f"SEV5 ticket successfully created for TACACS removal: {response.json().get('ticket_id')}")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to create SEV5 ticket for TACACS: {e}")


def main():
    """ Main function for the separation script. """
    logging.info("########### SEPARATION SCRIPT #############")
    operatorUN = get_user_input("Enter your LDAP username: ")
    operatorPass = getpass.getpass("Enter your LDAP password: ")

    # Gather usernames to be separated
    sepList = get_user_input("Enter LDAP user(s) to be separated (comma-separated): ").split(',')

    # Check if user is a vendor
    while True:
        isVendor = get_user_input("Is this user a vendor? (yes/no): ").lower()
        if isVendor in ('yes', 'no'):
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'yes' or 'no'.")

    vendorEmail = None
    if isVendor == "yes":
        if any(sys in ACCESS_LIST for sys in ["PagerDuty", "Microsites"]):
            vendorEmail = get_user_input("Enter vendor email address: ")
        else:
            logging.info("Vendor email not needed for selected systems.")

    # Ask if we are checking or removing access
    while True:
        accessChoice = get_user_input("Would you like to remove all found access or just check access? (Remove/Check): ").lower()
        if accessChoice in ('remove', 'check'):
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'Remove' or 'Check'.")
    
    creds = {
        "operatorUN": operatorUN,
        "operatorPass": operatorPass,
        "sepList": sepList,
        "accessChoice": accessChoice,
        "vendorEmail": vendorEmail,
        "MOCK_MODE": MOCK_MODE  # 🟢 Global Mock Mode Toggle CLI Controlled
    }

    try:
        ldp = Connection(server, user=LDAP_BINDDN.format(user=operatorUN), password=operatorPass, auto_bind=True)
    except LDAPBindError:
        logging.error("❌ LDAP authentication failed. Invalid username or password.")
        return
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"⚠️ Unexpected LDAP error: {e}")
        return
    
    with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=5) as executor:
        executor.map(lambda user: process_user(ldp, user, creds), sepList)

    logging.info(f"####### No further access found for {user} #######")
    
    if MISSING_SCRIPTS:
        logging.warning(f"Missing separation scripts: {', '.join(set(MISSING_SCRIPTS))}")


def process_user(ldp, user, creds):
    """Process separation for an individual user."""
    try:
        logging.info(f"Processing user: {user}")
        if "MOCK_MODE" in creds and creds["MOCK_MODE"]:
            logging.info(f"[MOCK] Simulating access removal for {user}.")
            return
        
        check_rt_for_access_tickets(user)
        if ldapQuery(ldp, user):
            checkAccess(user, creds)
        check_high_priority_contact_list(user)
        if "TACACS" in ACCESS_LIST:
            submit_sev5_ticket_for_TACACS(user)
        logging.info(f"####### No further access found for {user} #######")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error processing user {user}: {e}")


def ldapQuery(ldp, user):
    """Check if user exists in LDAP."""
    logging.info(f"Checking LDAP access for {user}...")

    try:
        ldp.search(LDAP_BASEDN, f"(cn={user})", ldap.SUBTREE)
        if not ldp.entries:
            logging.warning(f"User {user} not found in LDAP.")
            return False
        return True
    except ldap.LDAPException as e:
        logging.error(f"LDAP query failed for {user}: {e}")
        return False


def checkAccess(user, creds):
    """Run access removal scripts."""
    global MISSING_SCRIPTS 
    logging.info(f"Checking access for {user}...")
    for system in ACCESS_LIST:
        try:
            sep_module = __import__(f"separations.{system.lower()}", fromlist=[""])
            sep_module.main(user, creds)
        except ImportError:
            MISSING_SCRIPTS.append(system)
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"Error running {system} separation: {e}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

SOC SOP newHireTickets
SOC SOP newHireTickets
Jump to navigationJump to search


Handling Incoming New Hire TicketsNew Marchex EmployeeNew Marchex VendorNew vendor-SOC EmployeeNew SOC Employee


Purpose of this document:

This is a basic check sheet for new hires that will be working in the SOC. This will get them provisioned with the proper permissions. If we miss something PLEASE make sure you add it.





SOC Operator working the NEW HIRE Ticket


This portion is for the SOC operator who owns the New SOC User's ticket.



1. (CURRENTLY NOT TO DO WHILE THIS IS FIGURED OUT)Verify the user in in the "soc security group" in for access to the soc share. If they cannot access the SOC share, send mail to the SOC Manager and get them access to it by adding them to the SOC security group.

\\marchex\files\soc

2. Create a reminder on the SOC calendar for 90 days after the start date, to cut a ticket to Net-Eng requesting tacacs access

3. (CURRENTLY vendor-soc will not be doing onboarding/offboarding) Send an email to the SOC manager, and ask for the user to be added to the 'soc-operations' group in RT.

4.Create an AWS account for the new SOC operator, mirroring an existing SOC operator's permissions (infrastructure-aws)

5. Grant accounts to the user on OPNEXT and OPTLDM, and then create a ticket with DBAs to grant special SOC permissions.

6. Update add user to databag_soc_alerta so they have access to alerta .

7. Grant the operator access to [Jira]

8. Grant the operator access to the following Security groups in Last 3.

sysadmin
soc-admin
last-admin


9. (This access should be part of newhire/separation and for now will not be granted) Grant the operator access to the following item in [MI5]:

dcm_reports: report_viewer
ism: context_admin
arc: arc_ui_access
asq: Admin


10. Grant the operator access in [Slack].

11. Grant the operator ops-sudo by using [this repo].

12. Cut a request ticket to the Tools team to get the user a "Private key" for chef/knife.

13. Cut a request ticket to the SOC Manager to add the user to the SOC-Operators DL

14. Cut a request ticket to CORP IT asking for access to Directory Manager.

SOC SOP newHireTickets
SOC SOP newHireTickets
Jump to navigationJump to search


Handling Incoming New Hire TicketsNew Marchex EmployeeNew Marchex VendorNew vendor-SOC EmployeeNew SOC Employee
Set up the ticket to be worked
NOTE: New Hire tickets should never be taken out of the "SOC Employee Actions" queue under any circumstance.

Set-up ticket by setting the following fields
Escalation: None
Severity: 5
Tickettype: Request
Two-Way Contact: None
Product/service: SOC
Queue: SOC Employee Actions (should already be set to this, do not change it)
Message: SOP: https://wiki.marchex.com/index.php/SOC_SOP_newHireTickets
Status: Open
Confirm that there is SOC access to be granted. Check the following lines specifically but also read through the ticket to make sure there isn't a misplaced access request:
 -JIRA ACCOUNT?
 -ANY NON-STANDARD ACCESS [e.g., Adtrack, GitHub, QA]? [If YES, specify access and existing user permissions to emulate, if applicable (Adtrack: Mary Jones; QA: Bill Smith)]
If there is no access to grant, close the ticket with the message:
 No SOC access to grant.
Othwerise, continue.

Hand the ticket off to night shift. Currently give all tickets to Kamran and he will distribute them.

=============================================
Validate access to be granted:
For any access that needs to be granted, confirm that there is an existing employee to mirror (where necessary). If there is not, email the direct manager listed in the ticket requesting one.
If the ticket asks to mirror all of the access of an existing employee, audit that employee's access using the "check" option on the separation script to determine what needs to be granted: https://wiki.marchex.com/index.php/SOC_SOP_PROC_employeeSeparations
List all access to be granted in a new comment in the ticket. This can be done via the separation script printing the access of the person being mirrored.
Immediate or Backdated Hires
Every new hire creates three tickets. One comes to us in the Employee Actions Queue, one goes to Facilities, and one goes to Helpdesk. We can't grant any access to a new hire until their LDAP is created, which is done as part of the Helpdesk ticket. When we receive a new hire ticket that needs to be worked as soon as possible, follow the procedure below:

Search RT for the employee's name exactly as it appears in the title of the ticket. You should see all three new hire tickets in the results (one of which is your ticket in the SOC Employee Actions queue)
Click the ticket in the "Employee Actions" queue. This will open the ticket owned by CORP IT.
Look in that ticket for a comment that says something like "created user account"
If this comment exists, it has all the info you need (LDAP, email, etc) and the ticket can be worked. Proceed to the tab appropriate for the type of employee being hired.
If they haven't been added to LDAP, you can't work the ticket yet. Add a note to the ticket that Corp IT hasn't added them to LDAP yet so you can't proceed.

SOC SOP newHireTickets
SOC SOP newHireTickets
Jump to navigationJump to search


Handling Incoming New Hire TicketsNew Marchex EmployeeNew Marchex VendorNew vendor-SOC EmployeeNew SOC Employee
Description
Policy on how to handle New Hire tickets in the SOC employee action queue.

For new hire tickets No Additional Authorizations are needed as the manager was involved in the creation of the ticket, authorization is implied. Please note this is only for manager-level authorizations. If you see something that requires approval from a Director or a VP, then get the appropriate approval.

____________

Confirm the user has an LDAP set up following the instructions on the "Handling Incoming New Hire Tickets" tab
Grant any permissions listed Using normal access procedures
If clarification is needed regarding permissions, send an email to the direct manager listed in the ticket.
If the new user is a dev, give them libvirtd access following these instructions: https://wiki.marchex.com/index.php/SOC_SOP_KVM_Virsh_libvirtd#tab=Granting_Access
In the cases where access needs to be granted by another team, create a separate ticket and link the two tickets. Keep the original New Hire Ticket, and pass the other ticket to the team who will be granting the access.
When you are finished with the ticket, send an email to the new user outlining the access that they have. Users have no visibility into the ticket so they're often in the dark due to lack of communication, and assume they do not have access.

__NOTOC__

Handling Incoming New Hire Tickets
Set up the ticket to be worked
NOTE: New Hire tickets should never be taken out of the "SOC Employee
Actions" queue under any circumstance.

Set-up ticket by setting the following fields

Escalation: None
Severity: 5
Tickettype: Request
Two-Way Contact: None
Product/service: SOC
Queue: SOC Employee Actions (should already be set to this, do
not change it)
Message: SOP:
https://wiki.marchex.com/index.php/SOC_SOP_newHireTickets 
Status: Open
Confirm that there is SOC access to be granted. Check the following
lines specifically but also read through the ticket to make sure
there isn't a misplaced access request:
-JIRA ACCOUNT?
-ANY NON-STANDARD ACCESS [e.g., Adtrack, GitHub, QA]? [If YES, specify access and existing user permissions to emulate, if applicable (Adtrack: Mary Jones; QA: Bill Smith)]

If there is no access to grant, close the ticket with the message:
No SOC access to grant.

Othwerise, continue.

Hand the ticket off to night shift. Currently give all tickets to
Kamran and he will distribute them.

=========================================================

Validate access to be granted:

For any access that needs to be granted, confirm that there is
an existing employee to mirror (where necessary). If there is
not, email the direct manager listed in the ticket requesting
one.
If the ticket asks to mirror all of the access of an existing
employee, audit that employee's access using the "check" option
on the separation script to determine what needs to be granted:
https://wiki.marchex.com/index.php/SOC_SOP_PROC_employeeSeparations 
List all access to be granted in a new comment in the ticket. This
can be done via the separation script printing the access of the
person being mirrored.

Immediate or Backdated Hires
Every new hire creates three tickets. One comes to us in the Employee
Actions Queue, one goes to Facilities, and one goes to Helpdesk. We
can't grant any access to a new hire until their LDAP is created, which
is done as part of the Helpdesk ticket. When we receive a new hire
ticket that needs to be worked as soon as possible, follow the procedure
below:

Search RT for the employee's name exactly as it appears in the title
of the ticket. You should see all three new hire tickets in the
results (one of which is your ticket in the SOC Employee Actions
queue)
Click the ticket in the "Employee Actions" queue. This will open the
ticket owned by CORP IT.
Look in that ticket for a comment that says something like "created
user account"
If this comment exists, it has all the info you need (LDAP, email,
etc) and the ticket can be worked. Proceed to the tab appropriate
for the type of employee being hired.
If they haven't been added to LDAP, you can't work the ticket yet.
Add a note to the ticket that Corp IT hasn't added them to LDAP yet
so you can't proceed.

Grant any permissions listed Using normal access
procedures
If clarification is needed regarding permissions, send an email

If the new user is a dev, give them libvirtd access following these
instructions:
https://wiki.marchex.com/index.php/SOC_SOP_KVM_Virsh_libvirtd#tab=Granting_Access 
In the cases where access needs to be granted by another team,
create a separate ticket and link the two tickets. Keep the original
New Hire Ticket, and pass the other ticket to the team who will be

SOC SOP userAccessRequests

Follow
0

Edit

Dean Van Vlack
Mar 4
User Access Requests
====The following are done by CORP IT and not the SOC====

Hardware issues (laptops) or anything else that is non-production
LDAP issues
Marchex email accounts
Passwords for ldap accounts (soc can also do this)
Recurly
RT (but we can add people if we need to, see instructions below in
the UI section)
Smartsheet
Tableau and Tableau Desktop
VPN
The following are done by Infra Team and not the SOC
S3 (AWS)
Mind+ (MindSage) AWS Dev Instance - Sev 5 ticket to Infra Manager
Vlad
The following is currently done by the Data Platform on-call and can be passed to them
Confluent Cloud
The following is currently done by project owners
Rancher - Per Jason Peck: You login to rancher using LDAP, but
access to projects is given by project owners. Direct people making
access requests to request access from the project owners. If they
are asking for a product list, that is a read-only account which is
still granted by the project's owner.
Salesforce, SalesLoft, SalesIntel, and SalesNavigator - Adam Lindsey
is the account administrator and should be contacted for account
creation and also for support.
Engage/Spotlight account problems or special permissions go to Engage Platform (formerly known as One UI or Sales Edge UI)
Fortellis / eLead - Andy Thomson or Scott Foley can probably help
with this. eLead and Nexla are the big two automotive CRM tools. Spotlight integrates call data to them.
iDashboard - Per Kevin Gunaratnam: iDashboard to Kim Norwood.
Becoming On-call
If you get a request that someone just generally says they need the
appropriate access to become on-call for X team, follow this
SOP 
==Notes for tickets:== When you send a request for approvals, update the
ticket and send the people an email as well.

People don't always see RT emails or ignore them.

Update the ticket title to make it easier to read.
Access Request: <UI/tool/etc> for <User Name> or <Multi User> (if there are a bunch of users in the ticket)
(Note: using a '-' character will break searching for the RT ticket)

If it needs to have a removal date
add in the title : remove <Date>

Always put in a lot of notes to why you are potentially stalling a
ticket so they know what is going on.
Best Practice: Give these tickets 1 day to sit in stalled while they
wait. After that, you should resend the who ever we are waiting on.
Document the ticket well, so others in the SOC know what is going on and
the ticket creator too.

====The following do not require logins==== wiki.marchex.com  - uses LDAP
and does not require permissions to be granted
Nagios - does not require access or logins
Jenkins - This access is granted by last3 groups (toolsjenkins-dev)

Description
This SOP outlines the processes required to grant access to the many
UI's, tools, servers, and databases we support.

Vendor Access
Vendor account access is handled in the same way an FTE or Contractor is
handled with the exception that the Marchex contact responsible for the
vendor relation may not be the same as the technical/business contact
requesting access for the user.

Telmetrics/Callcap Access
All access approval should be granted by the MOC and no one else at this
time.

====Approvals Required====

Dev Managers CANNOT approve Sudo or Change Control requests even if
they are MOC. Only Vlad and Matt (and those designated by them) may
approve these items.

Environment

Access Requested

Approval Required

Production

Database Write

CC Approval

Production Server

Sudo / Root

CC Approval

Production Server

Read-Only, Read-Only database

No approval required

QA, DEVINT, and CorpIT (not include Tools QA hosts)

All

No Approval required

Production UI Access (Including Tableau)

All

Users Manager*

Production UI (Write/Publish)

Tableau

Ryley Whitaker

Non Production UI's

Most (excludes Change Control Approvers, Administrator)

No Approval Required

ARC (aka DCM UIv2)

If user has a Next account no further authorization required

An approved CC card does not implicitly grant permission. If
someone needs further permission to do a deploy, they must go
through the usual access request process. This is also not a
wake-up-able issue
Any requests from employees that are VP or C-level do not need any
manager approval.
While waiting for replies, set owner to Nobody, status to Stalled,
and admin-cc soc@marchex.com, assuming there are no further actions
you can take on the ticket.
Adtrack UI now has specific escalation instructions for Staff
level access.
For Site24x7 access email Soc-leadership@marchex.com . Pass the
ticket to the Soc Lead.
*Nagios does not require access or logins

===Steps to Give Users Access(By Product/Tool/Environment)===
====Host Access====

Follow the steps outlined in the Host Access
SOP
SOM1, SAD, QA, DEVINT - SSH/Root Access

SEA, Windows - CorpIt Access
KVM Sudo access
Databag updates
Virsh libvirt

====DB Access====

List of DB hosts:

MySQL hosts: http://wiki.marchex.com/index.php/SOC_SOP_DBMySQL
'''MSQL
Hosts''' 

Customrptdb, evo db, qa evo db, Healthdb, jandb, jatdb, jtndb, mercurydb, micrositedb, QA micrositedb, mysql-adhocdb, 
Mcsandboxdb, openserdb, pagedb, elpagedb, QA pagedb, PFCCAN DB, slingshotdb, QA slingshotdb, sundb, tangodb, QA tangodb

Oracle Hosts: http://wiki.marchex.com/index.php/SOC_SOP_DBOracle

import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
import subprocess

# 🔧 Define functions for each button action
def run_separations():
    messagebox.showinfo("SOC Tool", "Running separations script...")
    subprocess.run(["python", "separations.py"])  # Update with actual script name

def run_new_hires():
    messagebox.showinfo("SOC Tool", "Running new hire onboarding script...")
    subprocess.run(["python", "newhire.py"])  # Update with actual script name

def clear_rt_queue():
    messagebox.showinfo("SOC Tool", "Clearing SOC RT queue...")
    subprocess.run(["python", "close_cleared_rts.py"])  # Update with actual script name

# 🔲 Create the GUI window
root = tk.Tk()
root.title("SOC Tool")
root.geometry("400x300")
root.resizable(False, False)

# 🔹 Header Label
label = tk.Label(root, text="Marchex SOC Tool", font=("Arial", 16, "bold"))
label.pack(pady=20)

# 🔹 Buttons
btn_separations = tk.Button(root, text="Separations", font=("Arial", 12), command=run_separations, width=20, height=2)
btn_separations.pack(pady=10)

btn_new_hires = tk.Button(root, text="Give Access", font=("Arial", 12), command=run_new_hires, width=20, height=2)
btn_new_hires.pack(pady=10)

btn_clear_rt = tk.Button(root, text="Auto Clear RT Queue", font=("Arial", 12), command=clear_rt_queue, width=20, height=2)
btn_clear_rt.pack(pady=10)

# 🔹 Run the application
root.mainloop()

import logging
import getpass
import ldap3 as ldap
import sys
import os
import ssl
import requests

sys.path.append(os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/lib/python"))

import utils 
import rt_marchex as rt
from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor
from ldap3 import Server, Connection, Tls, ALL
from ldap3.core.exceptions import LDAPBindError


# Setup logging     
logging.basicConfig(
    format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s',
    level=logging.INFO
)

# 🟢 Mock Mode (Secret Backdoor Enabled)
MOCK_MODE = False  # Default is OFF

# 🔐 Secret Backdoor Command (Toggle Mock Mode)
secret_command = getpass.getpass("Enter command or press Enter to continue: ").strip().lower()
if secret_command == "testmode":
    MOCK_MODE = True
    logging.warning("🚀 Test Mode Activated: Mock Mode is ENABLED.")
else:
    logging.info("Running in LIVE Mode.")

# Systems that require separation processing
SYSTEMS_CATALOG = {
    "AdTrack": True,
    "AFR": True,
    "Auth0": True,
    "Avenger": True,

    "XMSHammer": True
}

ACCESS_LIST = [system for system, enabled in SYSTEMS_CATALOG.items() if enabled]
MISSING_SCRIPTS = []

# LDAP Configurations
LDAP_HOST = 'ldap.sea.marchex.com'
LDAP_PORT = 636
LDAP_BASEDN = 'ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com'
LDAP_BINDDN = 'uid={user},ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com'
LDAP_SF = '(cn={user})'

# RT (Request Tracker) Configuration
RT_HOST = 'https://rt.marchex.com'
RT_URL = 'https://rt.marchex.com/REST/1.0'
RT_USER = "socbot"  # Replace with actual RT user
RT_PASS = "securepass"  # Replace with actual RT password

# High Priority Contact List Location
HIGH_PRI_FILE = r'\\marchex\files\soc\Emergency\High Priority Contact List\NOCHighPriorityContactList1.xlsx'


try:
    server = Server(LDAP_HOST, port=LDAP_PORT, use_ssl=True)
    logging.info(f"✅ Successfully connected to LDAP server: {LDAP_HOST}:{LDAP_PORT}")
except Exception as e:
    logging.error(f"❌ Failed to connect to LDAP server: {e}")
    sys.exit(1)


def get_user_input(prompt):
    """Wrapper for input to handle common input scenarios."""
    try:
        return input(prompt).strip()
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error getting user input: {e}")
        return None


def get_directory_info(user):
    """Query Directory Manager for user alias & manager name."""
    directory_url = f"https://directorymanager.marchex.com/api/user/{user}"
    try:
        response = requests.get(directory_url)
        response.raise_for_status()
        user_data = response.json()
        return user_data.get('alias', 'Unknown'), user_data.get('manager', 'Unknown')
    except Exception as e:
        logging.warning(f"Failed to retrieve Directory Manager info for {user}: {e}")
        return 'Unknown', 'Unknown'


def check_rt_for_access_tickets(user):
    """Check RT (Request Tracker) for past access requests related to this user."""
    logging.info(f"Checking RT for past access requests related to {user}...")
    query = f"Owner = '{user}' AND (Status = 'new' OR Status = 'open')"
    tracker = rt.Rt(RT_URL, RT_USER, RT_PASS)
    if not tracker.login():
        logging.error("Failed to authenticate with RT.")
        return
    try:
        tickets = tracker.search(Queue="SOC", raw_query=query)
        if tickets:
            logging.info(f"User {user} has {len(tickets)} past access tickets in RT.")
            for ticket in tickets:
                logging.info(f"RT Ticket Found: {ticket['id']} - {ticket['Subject']}")
        else:
            logging.info(f"No previous access tickets found in RT for {user}.")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.warning(f"Error checking RT for {user}: {e}")


def check_high_priority_contact_list(user):
    """Check and remove user from High Priority Contact List."""
    if not os.path.exists(HIGH_PRI_FILE):
        logging.warning("High Priority Contact List file not found.")
        return
    try:
        wb = openpyxl.load_workbook(HIGH_PRI_FILE)
        sheet = wb.active
        for row in sheet.iter_rows():
            for cell in row:
                if str(user).lower() in str(cell.value).lower():
                    logging.info(f"Removing {user} from High Priority Contact List.")
                    cell.value = None
                    wb.save(HIGH_PRI_FILE)
                    return
        logging.info(f"{user} not found in High Priority Contact List.")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error modifying High Priority Contact List: {e}")


def submit_sev5_ticket_for_TACACS(user):
    """Submit a SEV5 ticket to NetEng for TACACS removal."""
    logging.info(f"Submitting SEV5 ticket for TACACS removal for {user}.")
    
    # Simulated API request
    ticket_payload = {
        "summary": f"SEV5 - Remove TACACS access for {user}",
        "description": f"User {user} requires TACACS access removal as part of separation.",
        "priority": "SEV5",
        "assigned_team": "NetEng"
    }
    try:
        response = requests.post("https://ticketing.marchex.com/api/tickets", json=ticket_payload)
        response.raise_for_status()
        logging.info(f"SEV5 ticket successfully created for TACACS removal: {response.json().get('ticket_id')}")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to create SEV5 ticket for TACACS: {e}")


def main():
    """ Main function for the separation script. """
    logging.info("########### SEPARATION SCRIPT #############")
    operatorUN = get_user_input("Enter your LDAP username: ")
    operatorPass = getpass.getpass("Enter your LDAP password: ")

    # Gather usernames to be separated
    sepList = get_user_input("Enter LDAP user(s) to be separated (comma-separated): ").split(',')

    # Check if user is a vendor
    while True:
        isVendor = get_user_input("Is this user a vendor? (yes/no): ").lower()
        if isVendor in ('yes', 'no'):
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'yes' or 'no'.")

    vendorEmail = None
    if isVendor == "yes":
        if any(sys in ACCESS_LIST for sys in ["PagerDuty", "Microsites"]):
            vendorEmail = get_user_input("Enter vendor email address: ")
        else:
            logging.info("Vendor email not needed for selected systems.")

    # Ask if we are checking or removing access
    while True:
        accessChoice = get_user_input("Would you like to remove all found access or just check access? (Remove/Check): ").lower()
        if accessChoice in ('remove', 'check'):
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'Remove' or 'Check'.")
    
    creds = {
        "operatorUN": operatorUN,
        "operatorPass": operatorPass,
        "sepList": sepList,
        "accessChoice": accessChoice,
        "vendorEmail": vendorEmail,
        "MOCK_MODE": MOCK_MODE  # 🟢 Global Mock Mode Toggle CLI Controlled
    }

    try:
        ldp = Connection(server, user=LDAP_BINDDN.format(user=operatorUN), password=operatorPass, auto_bind=True)
    except LDAPBindError:
        logging.error("❌ LDAP authentication failed. Invalid username or password.")
        return
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"⚠️ Unexpected LDAP error: {e}")
        return
    
    with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=5) as executor:
        executor.map(lambda user: process_user(ldp, user, creds), sepList)

    logging.info(f"####### No further access found for {user} #######")
    
    if MISSING_SCRIPTS:
        logging.warning(f"Missing separation scripts: {', '.join(set(MISSING_SCRIPTS))}")


def process_user(ldp, user, creds):
    """Process separation for an individual user."""
    try:
        logging.info(f"Processing user: {user}")
        if "MOCK_MODE" in creds and creds["MOCK_MODE"]:
            logging.info(f"[MOCK] Simulating access removal for {user}.")
            return
        
        check_rt_for_access_tickets(user)
        if ldapQuery(ldp, user):
            checkAccess(user, creds)
        check_high_priority_contact_list(user)
        if "TACACS" in ACCESS_LIST:
            submit_sev5_ticket_for_TACACS(user)
        logging.info(f"####### No further access found for {user} #######")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error processing user {user}: {e}")


def ldapQuery(ldp, user):
    """Check if user exists in LDAP."""
    logging.info(f"Checking LDAP access for {user}...")

    try:
        ldp.search(LDAP_BASEDN, f"(cn={user})", ldap.SUBTREE)
        if not ldp.entries:
            logging.warning(f"User {user} not found in LDAP.")
            return False
        return True
    except ldap.LDAPException as e:
        logging.error(f"LDAP query failed for {user}: {e}")
        return False


def checkAccess(user, creds):
    """Run access removal scripts."""
    global MISSING_SCRIPTS 
    logging.info(f"Checking access for {user}...")
    for system in ACCESS_LIST:
        try:
            sep_module = __import__(f"separations.{system.lower()}", fromlist=[""])
            sep_module.main(user, creds)
        except ImportError:
            MISSING_SCRIPTS.append(system)
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"Error running {system} separation: {e}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox, scrolledtext
import subprocess
import threading
import os

# ✅ Automatically detect the script location
SEPARATIONS_SCRIPT = os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/Separations/separation.py")

# Function to run the Separations process inside a new GUI window
def open_separations_window():
    sep_window = tk.Toplevel(root)
    sep_window.title("SOC - Separations")
    sep_window.geometry("500x500")

    # Header
    sep_label = tk.Label(sep_window, text="User Separations", font=("Arial", 14, "bold"))
    sep_label.pack(pady=10)

    # LDAP Username
    ldap_label = tk.Label(sep_window, text="Enter your LDAP username:")
    ldap_label.pack()
    ldap_entry = tk.Entry(sep_window, width=40)
    ldap_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Users to Separate
    users_label = tk.Label(sep_window, text="Enter LDAP user(s) to separate (comma-separated):")
    users_label.pack()
    users_entry = tk.Entry(sep_window, width=40)
    users_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Access Choice (Remove or Check)
    access_label = tk.Label(sep_window, text="Select action:")
    access_label.pack()
    access_choice = tk.StringVar(value="check")  # Default to "Check Access Only"
    access_check = tk.Radiobutton(sep_window, text="Check Access Only", variable=access_choice, value="check")
    access_remove = tk.Radiobutton(sep_window, text="Remove Access", variable=access_choice, value="remove")
    access_check.pack()
    access_remove.pack()

    # Mock Mode Toggle
    mock_mode = tk.BooleanVar(value=False)  # Default is OFF
    mock_checkbox = tk.Checkbutton(sep_window, text="Enable Mock Mode", variable=mock_mode)
    mock_checkbox.pack()

    # Log display area
    log_label = tk.Label(sep_window, text="Logs:")
    log_label.pack()
    log_area = scrolledtext.ScrolledText(sep_window, width=60, height=10)
    log_area.pack(pady=5)

    # Function to run the separations script
    def run_separations():
        ldap_user = ldap_entry.get().strip()
        users = users_entry.get().strip()
        action = access_choice.get()
        mock_flag = "--mock" if mock_mode.get() else ""

        if not ldap_user or not users:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "Please fill in all fields!")
            return

        log_area.insert(tk.END, f"🚀 Running separations script...\nMock Mode: {mock_mode.get()}\n")
        log_area.see(tk.END)

        def execute_script():
            try:
                result = subprocess.run(
                    ["python", "C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/Separations/separation.py", 
                     ldap_user, users, action, mock_flag], 
                    capture_output=True, text=True, check=True
                )
                log_area.insert(tk.END, result.stdout + "\n")
            except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
                log_area.insert(tk.END, f"❌ Error: {e.stderr}\n")

            log_area.see(tk.END)

        # Run in a separate thread to keep GUI responsive
        threading.Thread(target=execute_script, daemon=True).start()

    # Execute button
    run_btn = tk.Button(sep_window, text="Go", command=run_separations, font=("Arial", 12), width=20)
    run_btn.pack(pady=10)

    # Bind Enter key to execute function
    sep_window.bind('<Return>', lambda event: run_separations())

# Function to run New Hires script
def run_new_hires():
    messagebox.showinfo("SOC Tool", "Running new hire onboarding script...")
    subprocess.run(["python", "C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/Onboarding/newhire.py"])

# Function to run RT Queue Auto-Clear script
def clear_rt_queue():
    messagebox.showinfo("SOC Tool", "Clearing SOC RT queue...")
    subprocess.run(["python", "C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/Onboarding/close_cleared_rts.py"])

root = tk.Tk()
root.title("SOC Tool")
root.geometry("400x300")
root.resizable(False, False)

# 🔹 Header Label
label = tk.Label(root, text="Marchex SOC Tool", font=("Arial", 16, "bold"))
label.pack(pady=20)

# 🔹 Buttons
btn_separations = tk.Button(root, text="Separations", font=("Arial", 12), command=open_separations_window, width=20, height=2)
btn_separations.pack(pady=10)

btn_new_hires = tk.Button(root, text="Give Access", font=("Arial", 12), command=run_new_hires, width=20, height=2)
btn_new_hires.pack(pady=10)

btn_clear_rt = tk.Button(root, text="Auto Clear RT Queue", font=("Arial", 12), command=clear_rt_queue, width=20, height=2)
btn_clear_rt.pack(pady=10)

# 🔹 Run the application
root.mainloop()




import logging
import getpass
import ldap3 as ldap
import sys
import os
import ssl
import requests
import openpyxl
import json

sys.path.append(os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/lib/python"))

import utils 
import rt_marchex as rt
from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor
from ldap3 import Server, Connection, Tls, ALL
from ldap3.core.exceptions import LDAPBindError


# Setup logging     
logging.basicConfig(
    format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s',
    level=logging.INFO
)

# 🟢 Mock Mode (Secret Backdoor Enabled)
MOCK_MODE = False  # Default is OFF

# 🔐 Secret Backdoor Command (Toggle Mock Mode)
secret_command = getpass.getpass("Enter command or press Enter to continue: ").strip().lower()
if secret_command == "testmode":
    MOCK_MODE = True
    logging.warning("🚀 Test Mode Activated: Mock Mode is ENABLED.")
else:
    logging.info("Running in LIVE Mode.")

# Systems that require separation processing
SYSTEMS_CATALOG = {
    "AdTrack": True,
    "AFR": True,
    "Auth0": True,
    "Avenger": True,
    "AWS": True,
    "ADO": True,
    "AzurePortal": True,
    "CallScoring": True,
    "Chef": True,
    "Cuttlefish": True,
    "EmailAccess": True,
    "Engage": True,
    "EquityEdge_GreatPlains": True,
    "GitHub": True,
    "Grafana": True,
    "Ipplan": True,
    "JIRA": True,
    "Marchex.io": True,
    "MI5": True,
    "Microsites": True,
    "NewRelic": True,
    "Nexus": True,
    "NimUI": True,
    "NISMaps": True,
    "OpenVPN": True,
    "PagerDuty": True,
    "Pulley": True,
    "Postman": True,
    "RT": True, # Checking RT for past access requests
    "Slack": True,
    "MarketingEdge": True,
    "Sendgrid": True,
    "Sentry": True,
    "Snowflake": True,
    "TACACS": True,  # Needs special handling (SEV5 ticket)
    "Wallace": True,
    "XMSHammer": True
}

ACCESS_LIST = [system for system, enabled in SYSTEMS_CATALOG.items() if enabled]
MISSING_SCRIPTS = []

# LDAP Configurations
LDAP_HOST = 'ldap.sea.marchex.com'
LDAP_PORT = 636
LDAP_BASEDN = 'ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com'
LDAP_BINDDN = 'uid={user},ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com'
LDAP_SF = '(cn={user})'

# RT (Request Tracker) Configuration
RT_HOST = 'https://rt.marchex.com'
RT_URL = 'https://rt.marchex.com/REST/1.0'
RT_USER = "socbot"  # Replace with actual RT user
RT_PASS = "securepass"  # Replace with actual RT password

# High Priority Contact List Location
HIGH_PRI_FILE = r'\\marchex\files\soc\Emergency\High Priority Contact List\NOCHighPriorityContactList1.xlsx'


try:
    server = Server(LDAP_HOST, port=LDAP_PORT, use_ssl=True)
    logging.info(f"✅ Successfully connected to LDAP server: {LDAP_HOST}:{LDAP_PORT}")
except Exception as e:
    logging.error(f"❌ Failed to connect to LDAP server: {e}")
    sys.exit(1)


def get_user_input(prompt):
    """Wrapper for input to handle common input scenarios."""
    try:
        return input(prompt).strip()
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error getting user input: {e}")
        return None


def get_directory_info(user):
    """Query Directory Manager for user alias & manager name."""
    directory_url = f"https://directorymanager.marchex.com/api/user/{user}"
    try:
        response = requests.get(directory_url)
        response.raise_for_status()
        user_data = response.json()
        return user_data.get('alias', 'Unknown'), user_data.get('manager', 'Unknown')
    except Exception as e:
        logging.warning(f"Failed to retrieve Directory Manager info for {user}: {e}")
        return 'Unknown', 'Unknown'


def check_rt_for_access_tickets(user):
    """Check RT (Request Tracker) for past access requests related to this user."""
    logging.info(f"Checking RT for past access requests related to {user}...")
    query = f"Owner = '{user}' AND (Status = 'new' OR Status = 'open')"
    tracker = rt.Rt(RT_URL, RT_USER, RT_PASS)
    if not tracker.login():
        logging.error("Failed to authenticate with RT.")
        return
    try:
        tickets = tracker.search(Queue="SOC", raw_query=query)
        if tickets:
            logging.info(f"User {user} has {len(tickets)} past access tickets in RT.")
            for ticket in tickets:
                logging.info(f"RT Ticket Found: {ticket['id']} - {ticket['Subject']}")
        else:
            logging.info(f"No previous access tickets found in RT for {user}.")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.warning(f"Error checking RT for {user}: {e}")


def check_high_priority_contact_list(user):
    """Check and remove user from High Priority Contact List."""
    if not os.path.exists(HIGH_PRI_FILE):
        logging.warning("High Priority Contact List file not found.")
        return
    try:
        wb = openpyxl.load_workbook(HIGH_PRI_FILE)
        sheet = wb.active
        for row in sheet.iter_rows():
            for cell in row:
                if str(user).lower() in str(cell.value).lower():
                    logging.info(f"Removing {user} from High Priority Contact List.")
                    cell.value = None
                    wb.save(HIGH_PRI_FILE)
                    return
        logging.info(f"{user} not found in High Priority Contact List.")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error modifying High Priority Contact List: {e}")


def submit_sev5_ticket_for_TACACS(user):
    """Submit a SEV5 ticket to NetEng for TACACS removal."""
    logging.info(f"Submitting SEV5 ticket for TACACS removal for {user}.")
    
    # Simulated API request
    ticket_payload = {
        "summary": f"SEV5 - Remove TACACS access for {user}",
        "description": f"User {user} requires TACACS access removal as part of separation.",
        "priority": "SEV5",
        "assigned_team": "NetEng"
    }
    try:
        response = requests.post("https://ticketing.marchex.com/api/tickets", json=ticket_payload)
        response.raise_for_status()
        logging.info(f"SEV5 ticket successfully created for TACACS removal: {response.json().get('ticket_id')}")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to create SEV5 ticket for TACACS: {e}")


def main():
    """ Main function for the separation script. """
    logging.info("########### SEPARATION SCRIPT #############")
    operatorUN = get_user_input("Enter your LDAP username: ")
    operatorPass = getpass.getpass("Enter your LDAP password: ")

    # Gather usernames to be separated
    sepList = get_user_input("Enter LDAP user(s) to be separated (comma-separated): ").split(',')

    # Check if user is a vendor
    while True:
        isVendor = get_user_input("Is this user a vendor? (yes/no): ").lower()
        if isVendor in ('yes', 'no'):
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'yes' or 'no'.")

    vendorEmail = None
    if isVendor == "yes":
        if any(sys in ACCESS_LIST for sys in ["PagerDuty", "Microsites"]):
            vendorEmail = get_user_input("Enter vendor email address: ")
        else:
            logging.info("Vendor email not needed for selected systems.")

    # Ask if we are checking or removing access
    while True:
        accessChoice = get_user_input("Would you like to remove all found access or just check access? (Remove/Check): ").lower()
        if accessChoice in ('remove', 'check'):
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'Remove' or 'Check'.")
    
    creds = {
        "operatorUN": operatorUN,
        "operatorPass": operatorPass,
        "sepList": sepList,
        "accessChoice": accessChoice,
        "vendorEmail": vendorEmail,
        "MOCK_MODE": MOCK_MODE  # 🟢 Global Mock Mode Toggle CLI Controlled
    }

    try:
        ldp = Connection(server, user=LDAP_BINDDN.format(user=operatorUN), password=operatorPass, auto_bind=True)
    except LDAPBindError:
        logging.error("❌ LDAP authentication failed. Invalid username or password.")
        return
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"⚠️ Unexpected LDAP error: {e}")
        return
    
    with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=5) as executor:
        executor.map(lambda user: process_user(ldp, user, creds), sepList)

    logging.info(f"####### No further access found for {user} #######")
    
    if MISSING_SCRIPTS:
        logging.warning(f"Missing separation scripts: {', '.join(set(MISSING_SCRIPTS))}")


def process_user(ldp, user, creds):
    """Process separation for an individual user."""
    try:
        logging.info(f"Processing user: {user}")
        if "MOCK_MODE" in creds and creds["MOCK_MODE"]:
            logging.info(f"[MOCK] Simulating access removal for {user}.")
            return
        
        check_rt_for_access_tickets(user)
        if ldapQuery(ldp, user):
            checkAccess(user, creds)
        check_high_priority_contact_list(user)
        if "TACACS" in ACCESS_LIST:
            submit_sev5_ticket_for_TACACS(user)
        logging.info(f"####### No further access found for {user} #######")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error processing user {user}: {e}")


def ldapQuery(ldp, user):
    """Check if user exists in LDAP."""
    logging.info(f"Checking LDAP access for {user}...")

    try:
        ldp.search(LDAP_BASEDN, f"(cn={user})", ldap.SUBTREE)
        if not ldp.entries:
            logging.warning(f"User {user} not found in LDAP.")
            return False
        return True
    except ldap.LDAPException as e:
        logging.error(f"LDAP query failed for {user}: {e}")
        return False


def checkAccess(user, creds):
    """Run access removal scripts."""
    global MISSING_SCRIPTS 
    logging.info(f"Checking access for {user}...")
    for system in ACCESS_LIST:
        try:
            sep_module = __import__(f"separations.{system.lower()}", fromlist=[""])
            sep_module.main(user, creds)
        except ImportError:
            MISSING_SCRIPTS.append(system)
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"Error running {system} separation: {e}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

    """ Main function for the separation script. """
    logging.info("########### SEPARATION SCRIPT #############")
    operatorUN = get_user_input("Enter your LDAP username: ")
    operatorPass = getpass.getpass("Enter your LDAP password: ")

    # Gather usernames to be separated
    sepList = get_user_input("Enter LDAP user(s) to be separated (comma-separated): ").split(',')

    # Check if user is a vendor
    while True:

        if isVendor in ('yes', 'no'):
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'yes' or 'no'.")

        else:
            logging.info("Vendor email not needed for selected systems.")

    while True:
        accessChoice = get_user_input("Would you like to remove all found access or just check access? (Remove/Check): ").lower()
        if accessChoice in ('remove', 'check'):
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'Remove' or 'Check'.")
    
    creds = {
        "operatorUN": operatorUN,
        "operatorPass": operatorPass,
        "sepList": sepList,
        "accessChoice": accessChoice,
        "vendorEmail": vendorEmail,
        "MOCK_MODE": MOCK_MODE  # 🟢 Global Mock Mode Toggle CLI Controlled
    }

    try:
        ldp = Connection(server, user=LDAP_BINDDN.format(user=operatorUN), password=operatorPass, auto_bind=True)
    except LDAPBindError:
        logging.error("❌ LDAP authentication failed. Invalid username or password.")

        logging.warning(f"Missing separation scripts: {', '.join(set(MISSING_SCRIPTS))}")


def process_user(ldp, user, creds):
    """Process separation for an individual user."""
    try:
        logging.info(f"Processing user: {user}")
        if "MOCK_MODE" in creds and creds["MOCK_MODE"]:
            logging.info(f"[MOCK] Simulating access removal for {user}.")
            return
        
        check_rt_for_access_tickets(user)
        if ldapQuery(ldp, user):
            checkAccess(user, creds)
        check_high_priority_contact_list(user)
        if "TACACS" in ACCESS_LIST:
            submit_sev5_ticket_for_TACACS(user)
        logging.info(f"####### No further access found for {user} #######")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error processing user {user}: {e}")


def ldapQuery(ldp, user):
    """Check if user exists in LDAP."""
    logging.info(f"Checking LDAP access for {user}...")

    try:
        ldp.search(LDAP_BASEDN, f"(cn={user})", ldap.SUBTREE)
        if not ldp.entries:
            logging.warning(f"User {user} not found in LDAP.")
            return False
        return True
    except ldap.LDAPException as e:
        logging.error(f"LDAP query failed for {user}: {e}")
        return False


def checkAccess(user, creds):
    """Run access removal scripts."""
    global MISSING_SCRIPTS 
    logging.info(f"Checking access for {user}...")
    for system in ACCESS_LIST:
        try:
            sep_module = __import__(f"separations.{system.lower()}", fromlist=[""])
            sep_module.main(user, creds)
        except ImportError:
            MISSING_SCRIPTS.append(system)
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"Error running {system} separation: {e}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

import logging
import getpass
import ldap3 as ldap
import sys
import os
import ssl
import requests
import openpyxl
import json

sys.path.append(os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/lib/python"))

import utils 
import rt_marchex as rt
from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor
from ldap3 import Server, Connection, Tls, ALL
from ldap3.core.exceptions import LDAPBindError


# ✅ Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s',
    level=logging.INFO
)

# ✅ Read arguments from GUI (username, users, action, mock mode)
try:
    ldap_user = sys.argv[1]  # LDAP username
    users_to_separate = sys.argv[2].split(",")  # List of users
    action = sys.argv[3]  # "check" or "remove"
    MOCK_MODE = "--mock" in sys.argv  # If GUI sends --mock, enable mock mode
except IndexError:
    logging.error("❌ Error: Missing required arguments! Exiting...")
    sys.exit(1)

logging.info(f"🚀 Running separations script for: {users_to_separate}")
logging.info(f"🔍 Action: {'Check Access' if action == 'check' else 'Remove Access'}")
logging.info(f"🛠️ Mock Mode: {'ENABLED' if MOCK_MODE else 'DISABLED'}")

# ✅ LDAP Configuration
LDAP_HOST = 'ldap.sea.marchex.com'
LDAP_PORT = 636
LDAP_BASEDN = 'ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com'
LDAP_BINDDN = f'uid={ldap_user},ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com'

try:
    server = Server(LDAP_HOST, port=LDAP_PORT, use_ssl=True)
    ldp = Connection(server, user=LDAP_BINDDN, password=getpass.getpass("Enter your LDAP password: "), auto_bind=True)
    logging.info(f"✅ Successfully connected to LDAP server: {LDAP_HOST}")
except LDAPBindError:
    logging.error("❌ LDAP authentication failed. Invalid username or password.")
    sys.exit(1)
except Exception as e:
    logging.error(f"⚠️ Unexpected LDAP error: {e}")
    sys.exit(1)

# Systems that require separation processing
SYSTEMS_CATALOG = {
    "AdTrack": True,
    "AFR": True,
    "Auth0": True,
    "Avenger": True,
    "AWS": True,
    "ADO": True,
    "AzurePortal": True,

    "NimUI": True,
    "NISMaps": True,
    "OpenVPN": True,
    "PagerDuty": True,
    "Pulley": True,
    "Postman": True,
    "RT": True, # Checking RT for past access requests
    "Slack": True,
    "MarketingEdge": True,
    "Sendgrid": True,
    "Sentry": True,
    "Snowflake": True,
    "TACACS": True,  # Needs special handling (SEV5 ticket)
    "Wallace": True,
    "XMSHammer": True
}

ACCESS_LIST = [system for system, enabled in SYSTEMS_CATALOG.items() if enabled]
MISSING_SCRIPTS = []

# ✅ High Priority Contact List Location
HIGH_PRI_FILE = r'\\marchex\files\soc\Emergency\High Priority Contact List\NOCHighPriorityContactList1.xlsx'


try:
    server = Server(LDAP_HOST, port=LDAP_PORT, use_ssl=True)
    logging.info(f"✅ Successfully connected to LDAP server: {LDAP_HOST}:{LDAP_PORT}")
except Exception as e:
    logging.error(f"❌ Failed to connect to LDAP server: {e}")
    sys.exit(1)


def get_user_input(prompt):
    """Wrapper for input to handle common input scenarios."""
    try:
        return input(prompt).strip()
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error getting user input: {e}")
        return None


def get_directory_info(user):
    """Query Directory Manager for user alias & manager name."""
    directory_url = f"https://directorymanager.marchex.com/api/user/{user}"
    try:
        response = requests.get(directory_url)
        response.raise_for_status()
        user_data = response.json()
        return user_data.get('alias', 'Unknown'), user_data.get('manager', 'Unknown')
    except Exception as e:
        logging.warning(f"Failed to retrieve Directory Manager info for {user}: {e}")
        return 'Unknown', 'Unknown'


def check_rt_for_access_tickets(user):
    """Check RT (Request Tracker) for past access requests related to this user."""
    logging.info(f"Checking RT for past access requests related to {user}...")
    query = f"Owner = '{user}' AND (Status = 'new' OR Status = 'open')"
    tracker = rt.Rt(RT_URL, RT_USER, RT_PASS)
    if not tracker.login():
        logging.error("Failed to authenticate with RT.")
        return
    try:
        tickets = tracker.search(Queue="SOC", raw_query=query)
        if tickets:
            logging.info(f"User {user} has {len(tickets)} past access tickets in RT.")
            for ticket in tickets:
                logging.info(f"RT Ticket Found: {ticket['id']} - {ticket['Subject']}")
        else:
            logging.info(f"No previous access tickets found in RT for {user}.")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.warning(f"Error checking RT for {user}: {e}")


def check_high_priority_contact_list(user):
    """Check and remove user from High Priority Contact List."""
    if not os.path.exists(HIGH_PRI_FILE):
        logging.warning("High Priority Contact List file not found.")
        return
    try:
        wb = openpyxl.load_workbook(HIGH_PRI_FILE)
        sheet = wb.active
        for row in sheet.iter_rows():
            for cell in row:
                if str(user).lower() in str(cell.value).lower():
                    logging.info(f"Removing {user} from High Priority Contact List.")
                    cell.value = None
                    wb.save(HIGH_PRI_FILE)
                    return
        logging.info(f"{user} not found in High Priority Contact List.")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error modifying High Priority Contact List: {e}")


def submit_sev5_ticket_for_TACACS(user):
    """Submit a SEV5 ticket to NetEng for TACACS removal."""
    logging.info(f"Submitting SEV5 ticket for TACACS removal for {user}.")
    # Simulated API request
    ticket_payload = {
        "summary": f"SEV5 - Remove TACACS access for {user}",
        "description": f"User {user} requires TACACS access removal as part of separation.",
        "priority": "SEV5",
        "assigned_team": "NetEng"
    }
    try:
        response = requests.post("https://ticketing.marchex.com/api/tickets", json=ticket_payload)
        response.raise_for_status()
        logging.info(f"SEV5 ticket successfully created for TACACS removal: {response.json().get('ticket_id')}")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Failed to create SEV5 ticket for TACACS: {e}")


def main():
    """ Main function for the separation script. """
    logging.info("########### SEPARATION SCRIPT #############")
    operatorUN = get_user_input("Enter your LDAP username: ")
    operatorPass = getpass.getpass("Enter your LDAP password: ")

    # Gather usernames to be separated
    sepList = get_user_input("Enter LDAP user(s) to be separated (comma-separated): ").split(',')

    # Check if user is a vendor
    while True:
        isVendor = get_user_input("Is this user a vendor? (yes/no): ").lower()
        if isVendor in ('yes', 'no'):
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'yes' or 'no'.")

    vendorEmail = None
    if isVendor == "yes":
        if any(sys in ACCESS_LIST for sys in ["PagerDuty", "Microsites"]):
            vendorEmail = get_user_input("Enter vendor email address: ")
        else:
            logging.info("Vendor email not needed for selected systems.")

    # Ask if we are checking or removing access
    while True:
        accessChoice = get_user_input("Would you like to remove all found access or just check access? (Remove/Check): ").lower()
        if accessChoice in ('remove', 'check'):
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'Remove' or 'Check'.")
    
    creds = {
        "operatorUN": operatorUN,
        "operatorPass": operatorPass,
        "sepList": sepList,
        "accessChoice": accessChoice,
        "vendorEmail": vendorEmail,
        "MOCK_MODE": MOCK_MODE  # 🟢 Global Mock Mode Toggle CLI Controlled
    }

    try:
        ldp = Connection(server, user=LDAP_BINDDN.format(user=operatorUN), password=operatorPass, auto_bind=True)
    except LDAPBindError:
        logging.error("❌ LDAP authentication failed. Invalid username or password.")
        return
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"⚠️ Unexpected LDAP error: {e}")
        return
    
    with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=5) as executor:
        executor.map(lambda user: process_user(ldp, user, creds), sepList)

    logging.info(f"####### No further access found for {user} #######")
    
    if MISSING_SCRIPTS:
        logging.warning(f"Missing separation scripts: {', '.join(set(MISSING_SCRIPTS))}")


def process_user(user):
    """Process separation for an individual user."""
    try:
        logging.info(f"Processing user: {user}")
        if MOCK_MODE:
            logging.info(f"[MOCK] Simulating access removal for {user}.")
            return
        check_rt_for_access_tickets(user)
        if ldapQuery(ldp, user):
            for system in ACCESS_LIST:
                system_script = f"C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/Separations/{system.lower()}.py"
                if os.path.exists(system_script):
                    os.system(f'python "{system_script}" {user} {action} {"--mock" if MOCK_MODE else ""}')
                else:
                    logging.warning(f"⚠️ {system} script not found.")
        check_high_priority_contact_list(user)
        if "TACACS" in ACCESS_LIST:
            submit_sev5_ticket_for_TACACS(user)
        logging.info(f"✅ Completed processing for {user}")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error processing user {user}: {e}")


def ldapQuery(ldp, user):
    """Check if user exists in LDAP."""
    logging.info(f"Checking LDAP access for {user}...")
    try:
        ldp.search(LDAP_BASEDN, f"(cn={user})", ldap.SUBTREE)
        if not ldp.entries:
            logging.warning(f"User {user} not found in LDAP.")
            return False
        return True
    except ldap.LDAPException as e:
        logging.error(f"LDAP query failed for {user}: {e}")
        return False


def checkAccess(user, creds):
    """Run access removal scripts."""
    global MISSING_SCRIPTS 
    logging.info(f"Checking access for {user}...")
    for system in ACCESS_LIST:
        try:
            sep_module = __import__(f"separations.{system.lower()}", fromlist=[""])
            sep_module.main(user, creds)
        except ImportError:
            MISSING_SCRIPTS.append(system)
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"Error running {system} separation: {e}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox, scrolledtext
import subprocess
import threading
import os

# ✅ Automatically detect the script location
SEPARATIONS_SCRIPT = os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/Separations/separation.py")

# Function to run the Separations process inside a new GUI window
def open_separations_window():
    sep_window = tk.Toplevel(root)
    sep_window.title("SOC - Separations")
    sep_window.geometry("500x500")

    # Header
    sep_label = tk.Label(sep_window, text="User Separations", font=("Arial", 14, "bold"))
    sep_label.pack(pady=10)

    # LDAP Username
    ldap_label = tk.Label(sep_window, text="Enter your LDAP username:")
    ldap_label.pack()
    ldap_entry = tk.Entry(sep_window, width=40)
    ldap_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Users to Separate
    users_label = tk.Label(sep_window, text="Enter LDAP user(s) to separate (comma-separated):")
    users_label.pack()
    users_entry = tk.Entry(sep_window, width=40)
    users_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Access Choice (Remove or Check)
    access_label = tk.Label(sep_window, text="Select action:")
    access_label.pack()
    access_choice = tk.StringVar(value="check")  # Default to "Check Access Only"
    access_check = tk.Radiobutton(sep_window, text="Check Access Only", variable=access_choice, value="check")
    access_remove = tk.Radiobutton(sep_window, text="Remove Access", variable=access_choice, value="remove")
    access_check.pack()
    access_remove.pack()

    # Mock Mode Toggle
    mock_mode = tk.BooleanVar(value=False)  # Default is OFF
    mock_checkbox = tk.Checkbutton(sep_window, text="Enable Mock Mode", variable=mock_mode)
    mock_checkbox.pack()

    # Log display area
    log_label = tk.Label(sep_window, text="Logs:")
    log_label.pack()
    log_area = scrolledtext.ScrolledText(sep_window, width=60, height=10)
    log_area.pack(pady=5)

    # Function to run the separations script
    def run_separations():
        ldap_user = ldap_entry.get().strip()
        users = users_entry.get().strip()
        action = access_choice.get()
        mock_flag = "--mock" if mock_mode.get() else ""

        if not ldap_user or not users:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "Please fill in all fields!")
            return

        log_area.insert(tk.END, f"🚀 Running separations script...\nMock Mode: {mock_mode.get()}\n")
        log_area.see(tk.END)

        def execute_script():
            try:
                result = subprocess.run(
                    ["python", "C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/Separations/separation.py", 
                     ldap_user, users, action, mock_flag], 
                    capture_output=True, text=True, check=True
                )
                log_area.insert(tk.END, result.stdout + "\n")
            except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
                log_area.insert(tk.END, f"❌ Error: {e.stderr}\n")

            log_area.see(tk.END)

        # Run in a separate thread to keep GUI responsive
        threading.Thread(target=execute_script, daemon=True).start()

    # Execute button
    run_btn = tk.Button(sep_window, text="Go", command=run_separations, font=("Arial", 12), width=20)
    run_btn.pack(pady=10)

    # Bind Enter key to execute function
    sep_window.bind('<Return>', lambda event: run_separations())

# Function to run New Hires script
def run_new_hires():
    messagebox.showinfo("SOC Tool", "Running new hire onboarding script...")
    subprocess.run(["python", "C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/Onboarding/newhire.py"])

# Function to run RT Queue Auto-Clear script
def clear_rt_queue():
    messagebox.showinfo("SOC Tool", "Clearing SOC RT queue...")
    subprocess.run(["python", "C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/Onboarding/close_cleared_rts.py"])

# 🔲 Create the GUI window

root.mainloop()

Marchex Identity & Access Management Overview
This document should serve as an overview of the Identity & Access Management infrastructure at Marchex. This includes all Active Directory domains, OpenLDAP environments & how they all connect to each other.
If you'd like more information on the LDAP service/directory itself, please see the LDAP document.

Processes (READ THIS)
If you have ANY questions about these processes, please contact the IAM service owner, currently Tim Wiley (tim@marchex.com or tim@mim on MIM).

This is likely the most important part of this document because it's the most often ignored. Marchex's IAM infrastruture was created to meet controls set forth by SOX auditors.

The most important of these controls are as follows (these do not apply to service accounts):

User provisioning be closely controlled by an approver.
Depending on method, it may be a single approver or it may be a team of approvers.
Separated user accounts be automatically disabled across all environments.
User Provisioning
With the above mind, there is only one approved way to be granted access to ANY machine or service controlled by this system:

Last3 (Requires an RT Request)
To request access to Marchex resources, please submit a ticket to production-requests@marchex.com

If you are creating local accounts on machines or in LDAP/AD Domains, you're doing it wrong & you should stop immediately.

Environment Provisioning
To provision a new authentication environment (New AD/LDAP instance in a new data center), please contact the owner of the IAM services for consultation. This owner will need to configure things in the IAM system to handle accounts properly.

At the time of writing, that IAM service owner is Tim Wiley (tim@marchex.com or tim@mim on MIM).

If you are setting up AD/LDAP environments without including the IAM service owner, you're doing it wrong & you should stop immediately.

Infrastructure
Marchex Corporate Active Directory
Corp IT owns the corporate AD infrastructure (MARCHEX domain).
User accounts are created & managed here. This domain should be the definitive source of all account information.
Accounts are replicated to the NetIQ IDM cluster by way of the Remote Loader, a piece of NetIQ software that allows AD to interface with the IDM infrastructure. The Remote Loader runs on dc01sea.windows.
All MARCHEX domain controllers run another piece of NetIQ software called a password shim/filter that captures password changes & sends them to the remote loader prior to encryption. The remote loader then updates the user's password over a secure, encrypted connection to the directory.sea cluster.
Directory.sea (NetIQ Identity Manager/eDirectory Cluster)
Tim Wiley (tim@marchex.com or tim@mim on MIM) owns the directory.sea cluster
Composed of directory.sea (the VIP) & corpidm{1,2}.sea.
This cluster runs the NetIQ Identity Manager (version 4.7) & eDirectory (version 9.1) software & serves as the spoke in our "hub & spoke" IAM design.
NetIQ eDirectory serves as the directory service/data store for the IDM system. It provides an LDAP service among other lesser used services.
There exists a two-way replication of data between corpidm1.sea & corpidm2.sea.
NetIQ Identity Manager provides, most notably, the mechanism by which accounts are replicated from Marchex AD to all of the connected environments, whether they be Active Directory or OpenLDAP.
Part of the NetIQ IDM magic is a mechanism referred to as a "driver" that can interface with connected systems via LDAP (for OpenLDAP environments) or a remote loader (for AD environments). The drivers are configured to do a number of tasks including mapping attributes across systems, massaging the data based on defined custom rules, etc. The drivers are the components that allow disparate systems the ability to interface with each other.
The drivers run only on corpidm1.sea
It also provides NetIQ Certificate Server. We don't fully utilize it (we don't always verify certificate chains), but it was used to create MARCHEX_CA.pem as well as all of the LDAP server certificates.
NetIQ IDM & eDirectory can be managed/configured via iManager (hosted on both corpidm{1,2}.sea) or NetIQ Designer (a desktop application).
OpenLDAP Environments
ldap.sea
Composed of ldap.sea (the VIP) & ldap{1,2}.sea
The LDAP-SEA IDM driver pushes data to ldap1.sea.
ldap2.sea replicates data from ldap1.sea.
ldap.sad
Composed of ldap.sad (the VIP) & ldap{1,2}.sad
The LDAP-SAD IDM driver pushes data to ldap1.sad.
ldap2.sad replicates data from ldap1.sad.
ldap.sea1
Composed of ldap.sea1 (the VIP) & ldap{1,2}.sea1
The LDAP-SEA1 IDM driver pushes data to ldap1.sea1.
ldap2.sea1 replicates data from ldap1.sea1.
ldap.sea2
Composed of ldap{1,2}.sea2. The ldap.sea2 VIP doesn't yet exist.
The LDAP-SEA2 IDM driver pushes data to ldap1.sea2.
ldap2.sea2 replicates data from ldap1.sea2.
ldap.som1
Composed of ldap.som1 (the VIP) & ldap{1,2,3}.som1
The LDAP-SOM1 IDM driver pushes data to ldap1.som1.
ldap{2,3}.som1 replicate data from ldap1.som1.
ldap.qa
Composed of ldap.qa (the VIP) & qa-ldap{1,2}.sea1
The LDAP-QA IDM driver pushes data to qa-ldap1.sea1.
qa-ldap2.sea1 replicates data from qa-ldap1.sea1.
ldap.devint
Composed of ldap.devint (the VIP) & di-ldap{1,2}.sea1
The LDAP-DEVINT IDM driver pushes data to di-ldap1.sea1.
di-ldap2.sea1 replicates data from di-ldap1.sea1.
ldap.aws-us-east-1-vpc1
Composed of ldap.aws-us-east-1-vpc1 (the VIP) & ldap{1,2}.aws-us-east-1-vpc1
The LDAP-AWS-US-EAST-1-VPC1 IDM driver pushes data to ldap1.aws-us-east-1-vpc1.
ldap2.aws-us-east-1-vpc1 replicates data from ldap1.aws-us-east-1-vpc1.
ldap.aws-us-east-1-vpc3
Composed of ldap.aws-us-east-1-vpc3 (the VIP) & ldap{1,2}.aws-us-east-1-vpc3
The LDAP-AWS-US-EAST-1-VPC3 IDM driver pushes data to ldap1.aws-us-east-1-vpc3.
ldap2.aws-us-east-1-vpc3 replicates data from ldap1.aws-us-east-1-vpc3.
ldap.aws-us-west-2-vpc2
Composed of ldap.aws-us-west-2-vpc2 (the VIP) & ldap{1,2}.aws-us-west-2-vpc2
The LDAP-AWS-US-WEST-2-VPC2 IDM driver pushes data to ldap1.aws-us-west-2-vpc2.
ldap2.aws-us-west-2-vpc2 replicates data from ldap1.aws-us-west-2-vpc2.
ldap.aws-us-west-2-vpc4
Composed of ldap.aws-us-west-2-vpc4 (the VIP) & ldap{1,2}.aws-us-west-2-vpc4
The LDAP-AWS-US-WEST-2-VPC4 IDM driver pushes data to ldap1.aws-us-west-2-vpc4.
ldap2.aws-us-west-2-vpc4 replicates data from ldap1.aws-us-west-2-vpc4.
