import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox, scrolledtext
import subprocess
import threading
import os

# ✅ Automatically detect the script location
SEPARATIONS_SCRIPT = os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/Separations/separation.py")

# Function to run the Separations process inside a new GUI window
def open_separations_window():
    sep_window = tk.Toplevel(root)
    sep_window.title("SOC - Separations")
    sep_window.geometry("500x500")

    # Header
    sep_label = tk.Label(sep_window, text="User Separations", font=("Arial", 14, "bold"))
    sep_label.pack(pady=10)

    # LDAP Username
    ldap_label = tk.Label(sep_window, text="Enter your LDAP username:")
    ldap_label.pack()
    ldap_entry = tk.Entry(sep_window, width=40)
    ldap_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Users to Separate
    users_label = tk.Label(sep_window, text="Enter LDAP user(s) to separate (comma-separated):")
    users_label.pack()
    users_entry = tk.Entry(sep_window, width=40)
    users_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Access Choice (Remove or Check)
    access_label = tk.Label(sep_window, text="Select action:")
    access_label.pack()
    access_choice = tk.StringVar(value="check")  # Default to "Check Access Only"
    access_check = tk.Radiobutton(sep_window, text="Check Access Only", variable=access_choice, value="check")
    access_remove = tk.Radiobutton(sep_window, text="Remove Access", variable=access_choice, value="remove")
    access_check.pack()
    access_remove.pack()

    # Mock Mode Toggle
    mock_mode = tk.BooleanVar(value=False)  # Default is OFF
    mock_checkbox = tk.Checkbutton(sep_window, text="Enable Mock Mode", variable=mock_mode)
    mock_checkbox.pack()

    # Log display area
    log_label = tk.Label(sep_window, text="Logs:")
    log_label.pack()
    log_area = scrolledtext.ScrolledText(sep_window, width=60, height=10)
    log_area.pack(pady=5)

    # Function to run the separations script
    def run_separations():
        ldap_user = ldap_entry.get().strip()
        users = users_entry.get().strip()
        action = access_choice.get()
        mock_flag = "--mock" if mock_mode.get() else ""

        if not ldap_user or not users:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "Please fill in all fields!")
            return

        log_area.insert(tk.END, f"🚀 Running separations script...\nMock Mode: {mock_mode.get()}\n")
        log_area.see(tk.END)

        def execute_script():
            try:
                result = subprocess.run(
                    ["python", "C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/Separations/separation.py", 
                     ldap_user, users, action, mock_flag], 
                    capture_output=True, text=True, check=True
                )
                log_area.insert(tk.END, result.stdout + "\n")
            except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
                log_area.insert(tk.END, f"❌ Error: {e.stderr}\n")

            log_area.see(tk.END)

        # Run in a separate thread to keep GUI responsive
        threading.Thread(target=execute_script, daemon=True).start()

    # Execute button
    run_btn = tk.Button(sep_window, text="Go", command=run_separations, font=("Arial", 12), width=20)
    run_btn.pack(pady=10)

    # Bind Enter key to execute function
    sep_window.bind('<Return>', lambda event: run_separations())

# Function to run New Hires script
def run_new_hires():
    messagebox.showinfo("SOC Tool", "Running new hire onboarding script...")
    subprocess.run(["python", "C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/Onboarding/newhire.py"])

# Function to run RT Queue Auto-Clear script
def clear_rt_queue():
    messagebox.showinfo("SOC Tool", "Clearing SOC RT queue...")
    subprocess.run(["python", "C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/Onboarding/close_cleared_rts.py"])

# 🔲 Create the GUI window
root = tk.Tk()
root.title("SOC Tool")
root.geometry("400x300")
root.resizable(False, False)

# 🔹 Header Label
label = tk.Label(root, text="Marchex SOC Tool", font=("Arial", 16, "bold"))
label.pack(pady=20)

# 🔹 Buttons
btn_separations = tk.Button(root, text="Separations", font=("Arial", 12), command=open_separations_window, width=20, height=2)
btn_separations.pack(pady=10)

btn_new_hires = tk.Button(root, text="Give Access", font=("Arial", 12), command=run_new_hires, width=20, height=2)
btn_new_hires.pack(pady=10)

btn_clear_rt = tk.Button(root, text="Auto Clear RT Queue", font=("Arial", 12), command=clear_rt_queue, width=20, height=2)
btn_clear_rt.pack(pady=10)

# 🔹 Run the application
root.mainloop()

    ldap_pass_label.pack()

btn_clear_rt.pack(pady=10)

import logging
import getpass
import ldap3 as ldap
import sys
import os
import requests
import openpyxl
from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor
from ldap3 import Server, Connection, ALL
from ldap3.core.exceptions import LDAPBindError  # Move LDAPBindError import

# ✅ Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s',
    level=logging.INFO
)

# ✅ Detect if running from GUI (arguments passed) or CLI (no args)
GUI_MODE = len(sys.argv) > 1

# ✅ Read arguments from GUI
if GUI_MODE:
    try:
        ldap_user = sys.argv[1]  # LDAP username
        ldap_pass = sys.argv[2]  # LDAP password
        users_to_separate = sys.argv[3].split(",")  # List of users
        action = sys.argv[4]  # "check" or "remove"
        MOCK_MODE = "--mock" in sys.argv  # Mock mode flag
    except IndexError:
        logging.error("❌ Error: Missing required arguments! Exiting...")
        sys.exit(1)
else:
    # CLI Mode - Prompt for user input
    ldap_user = input("Enter your LDAP username: ").strip()
    users_to_separate = input("Enter LDAP user(s) to separate (comma-separated): ").strip().split(",")
    
    while True:
        action = input("Would you like to remove all found access or just check access? (remove/check): ").strip().lower()
        if action in ["remove", "check"]:
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'remove' or 'check'.")

    MOCK_MODE = input("Enable Mock Mode? (yes/no): ").strip().lower() == "yes"

# ✅ Log execution mode
logging.info(f"🚀 Running separations script for: {users_to_separate}")
logging.info(f"🔍 Action: {'Check Access' if action == 'check' else 'Remove Access'}")
logging.info(f"🛠️ Mock Mode: {'ENABLED' if MOCK_MODE else 'DISABLED'}")

# ✅ LDAP Configuration
LDAP_HOST = 'ldap.sea.marchex.com'
LDAP_PORT = 636
LDAP_BASEDN = 'ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com'
LDAP_BINDDN = f'uid={ldap_user},ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com'

try:
    server = Server(LDAP_HOST, port=LDAP_PORT, use_ssl=True)
    ldp = Connection(server, user=LDAP_BINDDN, password=getpass.getpass("Enter your LDAP password: "), auto_bind=True)
    logging.info(f"✅ Successfully connected to LDAP server: {LDAP_HOST}")
except LDAPBindError:
    logging.error("❌ LDAP authentication failed. Invalid username or password.")
    sys.exit(1)
except Exception as e:
    logging.error(f"⚠️ Unexpected LDAP error: {e}")
    sys.exit(1)

# ✅ Systems that require separation processing
SYSTEMS_CATALOG = {
    "AdTrack": True, "AFR": True, "Auth0": True, "Avenger": True, "AWS": True,
    "ADO": True, "AzurePortal": True, "CallScoring": True, "Chef": True, "Cuttlefish": True,
    "EmailAccess": True, "Engage": True, "EquityEdge_GreatPlains": True, "GitHub": True,
    "Grafana": True, "Ipplan": True, "JIRA": True, "Marchex.io": True, "MI5": True,
    "Microsites": True, "NewRelic": True, "Nexus": True, "NimUI": True, "NISMaps": True,
    "OpenVPN": True, "PagerDuty": True, "Pulley": True, "Postman": True, "RT": True,
    "Slack": True, "MarketingEdge": True, "Sendgrid": True, "Sentry": True,
    "Snowflake": True, "TACACS": True, "Wallace": True, "XMSHammer": True
}

ACCESS_LIST = [system for system, enabled in SYSTEMS_CATALOG.items() if enabled]
MISSING_SCRIPTS = []

# ✅ High Priority Contact List Location
HIGH_PRI_FILE = r'\\marchex\files\soc\Emergency\High Priority Contact List\NOCHighPriorityContactList1.xlsx'

def check_rt_for_access_tickets(user):
    """Check RT (Request Tracker) for past access requests related to this user."""
    logging.info(f"Checking RT for past access requests related to {user}...")
    logging.info(f"No previous access tickets found in RT for {user} (Mocked).")

def check_high_priority_contact_list(user):
    """Check and remove user from High Priority Contact List."""
    if not os.path.exists(HIGH_PRI_FILE):
        logging.warning("High Priority Contact List file not found.")
        return
    try:
        wb = openpyxl.load_workbook(HIGH_PRI_FILE)
        sheet = wb.active
        for row in sheet.iter_rows():
            for cell in row:
                if str(user).lower() in str(cell.value).lower():
                    logging.info(f"Removing {user} from High Priority Contact List.")
                    cell.value = None
                    wb.save(HIGH_PRI_FILE)
                    return
        logging.info(f"{user} not found in High Priority Contact List.")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error modifying High Priority Contact List: {e}")

def ldapQuery(ldp, user):
    """Check if user exists in LDAP."""
    logging.info(f"Checking LDAP access for {user}...")
    try:
        ldp.search(LDAP_BASEDN, f"(cn={user})", ldap.SUBTREE)
        if not ldp.entries:
            logging.warning(f"User {user} not found in LDAP.")
            return False
        return True
    except ldap.LDAPException as e:
        logging.error(f"LDAP query failed for {user}: {e}")
        return False

def process_user(user):
    """Process separation for an individual user."""
    try:
        logging.info(f"Processing user: {user}")
        if MOCK_MODE:
            logging.info(f"[MOCK] Simulating access removal for {user}.")
            return
        
        check_rt_for_access_tickets(user)
        if ldapQuery(ldp, user):
            for system in ACCESS_LIST:
                system_script = f"C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/Separations/{system.lower()}.py"
                if os.path.exists(system_script):
                    os.system(f'python "{system_script}" {user} {action} {"--mock" if MOCK_MODE else ""}')
                else:
                    logging.warning(f"⚠️ {system} script not found.")
        
        check_high_priority_contact_list(user)
        logging.info(f"✅ Completed processing for {user}")

    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error processing user {user}: {e}")

# ✅ Run Separation Process in Parallel
with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=5) as executor:
    executor.map(process_user, users_to_separate)

logging.info(f"✅ Separation process completed for: {users_to_separate}")
still nothing happening when i press enter and my gui go button is missing now




import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox, scrolledtext
import subprocess
import threading
import os

# ✅ Automatically detect the script location
SEPARATIONS_SCRIPT = os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/Separations/separation.py")

# Function to run the Separations process inside a new GUI window
def open_separations_window():
    sep_window = tk.Toplevel(root)
    sep_window.title("SOC - Separations")
    sep_window.geometry("500x500")

    # Header
    sep_label = tk.Label(sep_window, text="User Separations", font=("Arial", 14, "bold"))
    sep_label.pack(pady=10)

    # LDAP Username
    ldap_label = tk.Label(sep_window, text="Enter your LDAP username:")
    ldap_label.pack()
    ldap_entry = tk.Entry(sep_window, width=40)
    ldap_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # LDAP Password (hidden input)
    ldap_pass_label = tk.Label(sep_window, text="Enter your LDAP password:")
    ldap_pass_label.pack()
    ldap_pass_entry = tk.Entry(sep_window, width=40, show="*")  # Mask input
    ldap_pass_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Users to Separate
    users_label = tk.Label(sep_window, text="Enter LDAP user(s) to separate (comma-separated):")
    users_label.pack()
    users_entry = tk.Entry(sep_window, width=40)
    users_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Access Choice (Remove or Check)
    access_label = tk.Label(sep_window, text="Select action:")
    access_label.pack()
    access_choice = tk.StringVar(value="check")  # Default to "Check Access Only"
    access_check = tk.Radiobutton(sep_window, text="Check Access Only", variable=access_choice, value="check")
    access_remove = tk.Radiobutton(sep_window, text="Remove Access", variable=access_choice, value="remove")
    access_check.pack()
    access_remove.pack()

    # Mock Mode Toggle
    mock_mode = tk.BooleanVar(value=False)  # Default is OFF
    mock_checkbox = tk.Checkbutton(sep_window, text="Enable Mock Mode", variable=mock_mode)
    mock_checkbox.pack()

    # Log display area
    log_label = tk.Label(sep_window, text="Logs:")
    log_label.pack()
    log_area = scrolledtext.ScrolledText(sep_window, width=60, height=10)
    log_area.pack(pady=5)

    # Function to run the separations script
    def run_separations():
        ldap_user = ldap_entry.get().strip()
        ldap_pass = ldap_pass_entry.get().strip()
        users = users_entry.get().strip()
        action = access_choice.get()
        mock_flag = "--mock" if mock_mode.get() else ""

        if not ldap_user or not users:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "Please fill in all fields!")
            return

        log_area.insert(tk.END, f"🚀 Running separations script...\nMock Mode: {mock_mode.get()}\n")
        log_area.see(tk.END)

        def execute_script():
            try:
                result = subprocess.run(
                    ["python", SEPARATIONS_SCRIPT, ldap_user, ldap_pass, users, action, mock_flag], 
                    capture_output=True, text=True
                )
                log_area.insert(tk.END, result.stdout + "\n")
                log_area.insert(tk.END, result.stderr + "\n")  # Show errors in the GUI
            except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
                log_area.insert(tk.END, f"❌ Error: {e.stderr}\n")

            log_area.see(tk.END)

        # Run in a separate thread to keep GUI responsive
        threading.Thread(target=execute_script, daemon=True).start()

    # Execute button
    run_btn = tk.Button(sep_window, text="Go", command=run_separations, font=("Arial", 12), width=20)
    run_btn.pack(pady=10)

    # Bind Enter key to execute function
    sep_window.bind('<Return>', lambda event: run_separations())

# Function to run New Hires script
def run_new_hires():
    messagebox.showinfo("SOC Tool", "Running new hire onboarding script...")
    subprocess.run(["python", "C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/Onboarding/newhire.py"])

# Function to run RT Queue Auto-Clear script
def clear_rt_queue():
    messagebox.showinfo("SOC Tool", "Clearing SOC RT queue...")
    subprocess.run(["python", "C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/Onboarding/close_cleared_rts.py"])

# 🔲 Create the GUI window
root = tk.Tk()
root.title("SOC Tool")
root.geometry("400x300")
root.resizable(False, False)

# 🔹 Header Label
label = tk.Label(root, text="Marchex SOC Tool", font=("Arial", 16, "bold"))
label.pack(pady=20)

# 🔹 Buttons
btn_separations = tk.Button(root, text="Separations", font=("Arial", 12), command=open_separations_window, width=20, height=2)
btn_separations.pack(pady=10)

btn_new_hires = tk.Button(root, text="Give Access", font=("Arial", 12), command=run_new_hires, width=20, height=2)
btn_new_hires.pack(pady=10)

btn_clear_rt = tk.Button(root, text="Auto Clear RT Queue", font=("Arial", 12), command=clear_rt_queue, width=20, height=2)
btn_clear_rt.pack(pady=10)

# 🔹 Run the application
root.mainloop()

import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox, scrolledtext
import subprocess
import threading
import os

# ✅ Automatically detect the script location
SEPARATIONS_SCRIPT = os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/Separations/separation.py")

# Function to run the Separations process inside a new GUI window
def open_separations_window():
    sep_window = tk.Toplevel(root)
    sep_window.title("SOC - Separations")
    sep_window.geometry("525x550")

    # Header
    sep_label = tk.Label(sep_window, text="User Separations", font=("Arial", 14, "bold"))
    sep_label.pack(pady=10)

    # LDAP Username
    ldap_label = tk.Label(sep_window, text="Enter your LDAP username:")
    ldap_label.pack()
    ldap_entry = tk.Entry(sep_window, width=40)
    ldap_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # LDAP Password (hidden input)
    ldap_pass_label = tk.Label(sep_window, text="Enter your LDAP password:")
    ldap_pass_label.pack()
    ldap_pass_entry = tk.Entry(sep_window, width=40, show="*")  # Mask input
    ldap_pass_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Users to Separate
    users_label = tk.Label(sep_window, text="Enter LDAP user(s) to separate (comma-separated):")
    users_label.pack()
    users_entry = tk.Entry(sep_window, width=40)
    users_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Access Choice (Remove or Check)
    access_label = tk.Label(sep_window, text="Select action:")
    access_label.pack()
    access_choice = tk.StringVar(value="check")  # Default to "Check Access Only"
    access_check = tk.Radiobutton(sep_window, text="Check Access Only", variable=access_choice, value="check")
    access_remove = tk.Radiobutton(sep_window, text="Remove Access", variable=access_choice, value="remove")
    access_check.pack()
    access_remove.pack()

    # Mock Mode Toggle
    mock_mode = tk.BooleanVar(value=False)  # Default is OFF
    mock_checkbox = tk.Checkbutton(sep_window, text="Enable Mock Mode", variable=mock_mode)
    mock_checkbox.pack()

    # Log display area
    log_label = tk.Label(sep_window, text="Logs:")
    log_label.pack()
    log_area = scrolledtext.ScrolledText(sep_window, width=60, height=10)
    log_area.pack(pady=5)

    # Function to run the separations script
    def run_separations():
        ldap_user = ldap_entry.get().strip()
        ldap_pass = ldap_pass_entry.get().strip()
        users = users_entry.get().strip()
        action = access_choice.get()
        mock_flag = "--mock" if mock_mode.get() else ""

        if not ldap_user or not users:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "Please fill in all fields!")
            return

        log_area.insert(tk.END, f"🚀 Running separations script...\nMock Mode: {mock_mode.get()}\n")
        log_area.see(tk.END)

        def execute_script():
            try:
                result = subprocess.run(
                    ["python", SEPARATIONS_SCRIPT, ldap_user, ldap_pass, users, action, mock_flag], 
                    capture_output=True, text=True
                )
                log_area.insert(tk.END, result.stdout + "\n")
                log_area.insert(tk.END, result.stderr + "\n")  # Show errors in the GUI
            except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
                log_area.insert(tk.END, f"❌ Error: {e.stderr}\n")

            log_area.see(tk.END)

        # Run in a separate thread to keep GUI responsive
        threading.Thread(target=execute_script, daemon=True).start()

    # Execute button
    run_btn = tk.Button(sep_window, text="Execute", command=run_separations, font=("Arial", 12), width=20)
    run_btn.pack(pady=10) 

    # Bind Enter key to execute function
    sep_window.bind('<Return>', lambda event: run_separations())

# Function to run New Hires script
def run_new_hires():
    messagebox.showinfo("SOC Tool", "Running new hire onboarding script...")
    subprocess.run(["python", "C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/Onboarding/newhire.py"])

# Function to run RT Queue Auto-Clear script
def clear_rt_queue():
    messagebox.showinfo("SOC Tool", "Clearing SOC RT queue...")
    subprocess.run(["python", "C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/Onboarding/close_cleared_rts.py"])

# 🔲 Create the GUI window
root = tk.Tk()
root.title("SOC Tool")
root.geometry("400x300")
root.resizable(False, False)

# 🔹 Header Label
label = tk.Label(root, text="Marchex SOC Tool", font=("Arial", 16, "bold"))
label.pack(pady=20)

# 🔹 Buttons
btn_separations = tk.Button(root, text="Separations", font=("Arial", 12), command=open_separations_window, width=20, height=2)
btn_separations.pack(pady=10)

btn_new_hires = tk.Button(root, text="Give Access", font=("Arial", 12), command=run_new_hires, width=20, height=2)
btn_new_hires.pack(pady=10)

btn_clear_rt = tk.Button(root, text="Auto Clear RT Queue", font=("Arial", 12), command=clear_rt_queue, width=20, height=2)
btn_clear_rt.pack(pady=10)

# 🔹 Run the application
root.mainloop()

import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox, scrolledtext
import subprocess
import threading
import os

# ✅ Paths to scripts
SEPARATIONS_SCRIPT = os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/Separations/separation.py")
CHECK_SCRIPT = os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/Separations/check.py")
NEWHIRE_SCRIPT = os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/Onboarding/newhire.py")

# Function to run the Separations process inside a new GUI window
def open_separations_window():
    sep_window = tk.Toplevel(root)
    sep_window.title("SOC - Separations")
    sep_window.geometry("525x550")

    # Header
    sep_label = tk.Label(sep_window, text="User Separations", font=("Arial", 14, "bold"))
    sep_label.pack(pady=10)

    # LDAP Username
    ldap_label = tk.Label(sep_window, text="Enter your LDAP username:")
    ldap_label.pack()
    ldap_entry = tk.Entry(sep_window, width=40)
    ldap_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # LDAP Password (hidden input)
    ldap_pass_label = tk.Label(sep_window, text="Enter your LDAP password:")
    ldap_pass_label.pack()
    ldap_pass_entry = tk.Entry(sep_window, width=40, show="*")  # Mask input
    ldap_pass_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Users to Separate
    users_label = tk.Label(sep_window, text="Enter LDAP user(s) to separate (comma-separated):")
    users_label.pack()
    users_entry = tk.Entry(sep_window, width=40)
    users_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Mock Mode Toggle
    mock_mode = tk.BooleanVar(value=False)  # Default is OFF
    mock_checkbox = tk.Checkbutton(sep_window, text="Enable Mock Mode", variable=mock_mode)
    mock_checkbox.pack()

    # Log display area
    log_label = tk.Label(access_window, text="Logs:")
    log_label.pack()
    log_area = scrolledtext.ScrolledText(access_window, width=60, height=10)
    log_area.pack(pady=5)

    # Function to execute script with appropriate action
    def run_script(script_path, action):
        ldap_user = ldap_entry.get().strip()
        ldap_pass = ldap_pass_entry.get().strip()
        users = users_entry.get().strip()
        mock_flag = "--mock" if mock_mode.get() else ""

        if not ldap_user or not users:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "Please fill in all fields!")
            return

        log_area.insert(tk.END, f"🚀 Running {action} script...\nMock Mode: {mock_mode.get()}\n")
        log_area.see(tk.END)

        def execute():
            try:
                result = subprocess.run(
                    ["python", script_path, ldap_user, ldap_pass, users, action, mock_flag],
                    capture_output=True, text=True
                )
                log_area.insert(tk.END, result.stdout + "\n")
                log_area.insert(tk.END, result.stderr + "\n")
            except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
                log_area.insert(tk.END, f"❌ Error: {e.stderr}\n")
            log_area.see(tk.END)

        threading.Thread(target=execute, daemon=True).start()

    # Buttons for different actions
    btn_check_access = tk.Button(access_window, text="Check Access", font=("Arial", 12),
                                 command=lambda: run_script(CHECK_SCRIPT, "check"), width=20)
    btn_check_access.pack(pady=5)

    btn_give_access = tk.Button(access_window, text="Give Access", font=("Arial", 12),
                                command=lambda: run_script(NEWHIRE_SCRIPT, "give"), width=20)
    btn_give_access.pack(pady=5)

    btn_remove_access = tk.Button(access_window, text="Remove Access", font=("Arial", 12),
                                  command=lambda: run_script(SEPARATIONS_SCRIPT, "remove"), width=20)
    btn_remove_access.pack(pady=5)

# Function to run RT Queue Auto-Clear script
def clear_rt_queue():
    messagebox.showinfo("SOC Tool", "Clearing SOC RT queue...")
    subprocess.run(["python", "C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/Onboarding/close_cleared_rts.py"])

# 🔲 Create the GUI window
root = tk.Tk()
root.title("SOC Tool")
root.geometry("400x300")
root.resizable(False, False)

# 🔹 Header Label
label = tk.Label(root, text="Marchex SOC Tool", font=("Arial", 16, "bold"))
label.pack(pady=20)

# 🔹 Buttons
btn_user_access = tk.Button(root, text="User Access Management", font=("Arial", 12),
                            command=open_separations_window, width=25, height=2)
btn_user_access.pack(pady=10)

btn_clear_rt = tk.Button(root, text="Auto Clear RT Queue", font=("Arial", 12),
                         command=clear_rt_queue, width=25, height=2)
btn_clear_rt.pack(pady=10)

# 🔹 Run the application
root.mainloop()

import subprocess
import threading

import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox, scrolledtext
import subprocess
import threading
import os

# ✅ Paths to scripts
SEPARATIONS_SCRIPT = os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/Separations/separation.py")

import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox, scrolledtext
import subprocess
import threading
import os

# ✅ Paths to scripts
SEPARATIONS_SCRIPT = os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/socbot/separation.py")
CHECK_SCRIPT = os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/socbot/check.py")
giveaccess_SCRIPT = os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/socbot/giveaccess.py")
CLEAR_RT_SCRIPT = os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/socbot/close_cleared_rts.py")

# Function to run the Separations process inside a new GUI window
def open_separations_window():
    sep_window = tk.Toplevel(root)
    sep_window.title("SOC - Separations")
    sep_window.geometry("525x550")

    # Header
    sep_label = tk.Label(sep_window, text="User Separations", font=("Arial", 14, "bold"))
    sep_label.pack(pady=10)

    # LDAP Username
    ldap_label = tk.Label(sep_window, text="Enter your LDAP username:")
    ldap_label.pack()
    ldap_entry = tk.Entry(sep_window, width=40)
    ldap_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # LDAP Password (hidden input)
    ldap_pass_label = tk.Label(sep_window, text="Enter your LDAP password:")
    ldap_pass_label.pack()
    ldap_pass_entry = tk.Entry(sep_window, width=40, show="*")  # Mask input
    ldap_pass_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Users Field
    users_label = tk.Label(root, text="Enter LDAP user(s) (comma-separated):")
    users_label.pack()
    users_entry = tk.Entry(root, width=40)
    users_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Mock Mode Toggle
    mock_mode = tk.BooleanVar(value=False)  # Default is OFF
    mock_checkbox = tk.Checkbutton(sep_window, text="Enable Mock Mode", variable=mock_mode)
    mock_checkbox.pack()

    # Log display area
    log_label = tk.Label(sep_window, text="Logs:")
    log_label.pack()
    log_area = scrolledtext.ScrolledText(sep_window, width=60, height=10)
    log_area.pack(pady=5)

    # Function to run the separations script
    def run_separations():
        ldap_user = ldap_entry.get().strip()
        ldap_pass = ldap_pass_entry.get().strip()
        users = users_entry.get().strip()
        action = access_choice.get()
        mock_flag = "--mock" if mock_mode.get() else ""

        if not ldap_user or not users:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "Please fill in all fields!")
            return

        log_area.insert(tk.END, f"🚀 Running separations script...\nMock Mode: {mock_mode.get()}\n")
        log_area.see(tk.END)

        def execute():
            try:
                result = subprocess.run(
                    ["python", SEPARATIONS_SCRIPT, ldap_user, ldap_pass, users, action, mock_flag], 
                    capture_output=True, text=True
                )
                log_area.insert(tk.END, result.stdout + "\n")
                log_area.insert(tk.END, result.stderr + "\n")  # Show errors in the GUI
            except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
                log_area.insert(tk.END, f"❌ Error: {e.stderr}\n")

            log_area.see(tk.END)

        # Run in a separate thread to keep GUI responsive
        threading.Thread(target=execute, daemon=True).start()

    # Execute button
    run_btn = tk.Button(sep_window, text="Execute", command=run_separations, font=("Arial", 12), width=20)
    run_btn.pack(pady=10) 

    # Bind Enter key to execute function
    sep_window.bind('<Return>', lambda event: run_separations())

# Function to execute any script
def run_script(script_path, action):
    """Runs a script in a separate thread and logs output in a pop-up window."""
    execution_window = tk.Toplevel(root)
    execution_window.title(f"Running {action}")
    execution_window.geometry("500x400")
    log_area = scrolledtext.ScrolledText(execution_window, width=60, height=15)
    log_area.pack(pady=5)

    def execute():
        try:
            result = subprocess.run(["python", script_path], capture_output=True, text=True)
            log_area.insert(tk.END, result.stdout + "\n")
            log_area.insert(tk.END, result.stderr + "\n")
        except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
            log_area.insert(tk.END, f"❌ Error: {e.stderr}\n")
        log_area.see(tk.END)
    threading.Thread(target=execute, daemon=True).start()

root.title("SOC Tool")
root.geometry("400x300")
root.resizable(False, False)

import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox, scrolledtext
import subprocess
import threading
import os


# ✅ Paths to scripts
CHECK_ACCESS_SCRIPT = os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/socbot/checkaccess.py")
GIVE_ACCESS_SCRIPT = os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/socbot/giveaccess.py")
SEPARATIONS_SCRIPT = os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/socbot/separation.py")
CLEAR_RT_SCRIPT = os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/socbot/close_cleared_rts.py")


def open_action_window(action, script_path):
    """Opens a new window for the selected action (Check, Give, Remove Access)."""

    action_window = tk.Toplevel(root)
    action_window.title(f"SOC - {action} Access")
    action_window.geometry("500x500")

    tk.Label(action_window, text=f"{action} User Access", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=10)

    tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter your LDAP username:").pack()
    ldap_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    ldap_entry.pack(pady=5)

    tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter your LDAP password:").pack()
    ldap_pass_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40, show="*")  # Hide password input
    ldap_pass_entry.pack(pady=5)

    tk.Label(action_window, text=f"Enter LDAP username to {action.lower()} access for:").pack()
    target_user_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    target_user_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Mock Mode Toggle (for test mode)
    mock_mode = tk.BooleanVar(value=False)
    tk.Checkbutton(action_window, text="Enable Mock Mode", variable=mock_mode).pack()

    # Log display area
    tk.Label(action_window, text="Logs:").pack()
    log_area = scrolledtext.ScrolledText(action_window, width=60, height=10)
    log_area.pack(pady=5)

    def execute_action():
        ldap_user = ldap_entry.get().strip()
        ldap_pass = ldap_pass_entry.get().strip()
        target_user = target_user_entry.get().strip()
        mock_flag = "--mock" if mock_mode.get() else ""

        if not ldap_user or not ldap_pass or not target_user:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "All fields are required!")
            return

        log_area.insert(tk.END, f"🚀 Running {action} script for {target_user}...\n")
        log_area.see(tk.END)

        def execute():
            try:
                result = subprocess.run(
                    ["python", script_path, ldap_user, ldap_pass, target_user, mock_flag],
                    capture_output=True, text=True
                )
                log_area.insert(tk.END, result.stdout + "\n")
                log_area.insert(tk.END, result.stderr + "\n")
            except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
                log_area.insert(tk.END, f"❌ Error: {e.stderr}\n")
            log_area.see(tk.END)

        threading.Thread(target=execute, daemon=True).start()

    # Execute button
    run_btn = tk.Button(action_window, text="Execute", command=execute_action, font=("Arial", 12), width=20)
    run_btn.pack(pady=10)

    # Bind Enter key to execute function
    action_window.bind('<Return>', lambda event: execute_action())

# 🔲 Create the GUI window

import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox, scrolledtext
import subprocess
import threading
import os

# ✅ Paths to individual system access check scripts
SYSTEM_SCRIPTS = {
    "AWS": os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/socbot/check_aws.py"),
    "JIRA": os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/socbot/check_jira.py"),
    "PagerDuty": os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/socbot/check_pagerduty.py"),
    "Slack": os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/socbot/check_slack.py"),
    "GitHub": os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/socbot/check_github.py"),
    "Azure": os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/socbot/check_azure.py")
}

def open_check_access_window():
    """Opens a new window to check LDAP user access."""

    check_window = tk.Toplevel()
    check_window.title("Check User Access")
    check_window.geometry("500x400")

    tk.Label(check_window, text="Enter your LDAP username:").pack()
    ldap_entry = tk.Entry(check_window, width=40)
    ldap_entry.pack(pady=5)

    tk.Label(check_window, text="Enter your LDAP password:").pack()
    ldap_pass_entry = tk.Entry(check_window, width=40, show="*")
    ldap_pass_entry.pack(pady=5)

    tk.Label(check_window, text="Enter LDAP user to check:").pack()
    user_entry = tk.Entry(check_window, width=40)
    user_entry.pack(pady=5)

    log_label = tk.Label(check_window, text="Logs:")
    log_label.pack()
    log_area = scrolledtext.ScrolledText(check_window, width=60, height=10)
    log_area.pack(pady=5)

    def check_access():
        ldap_user = ldap_entry.get().strip()
        ldap_pass = ldap_pass_entry.get().strip()
        check_user = user_entry.get().strip()

        if not ldap_user or not ldap_pass or not check_user:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "All fields are required!")
            return

        log_area.insert(tk.END, f"🚀 Checking access for {check_user}...\n")
        log_area.see(tk.END)

        def execute_check(system, script_path):
            """Runs a check script for a system in a separate thread."""
            try:
                result = subprocess.run(
                    ["python", script_path, check_user, ldap_user, ldap_pass],
                    capture_output=True, text=True
                )
                log_area.insert(tk.END, f"{system}:\n{result.stdout}\n")
                log_area.insert(tk.END, result.stderr + "\n")
            except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
                log_area.insert(tk.END, f"❌ Error checking {system}: {e.stderr}\n")
            log_area.see(tk.END)

        # Run access checks in parallel
        for system, script in SYSTEM_SCRIPTS.items():
            threading.Thread(target=execute_check, args=(system, script), daemon=True).start()

    # Execute button
    run_btn = tk.Button(check_window, text="Execute", command=check_access, font=("Arial", 12), width=20)
    run_btn.pack(pady=10)

    # Bind Enter key
    check_window.bind('<Return>', lambda event: check_access())

import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox, scrolledtext
import subprocess
import threading
import os

# ✅ Paths to individual system check scripts
SYSTEM_SCRIPTS = {
    "AWS": os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/socbot/check_aws.py"),
    "JIRA": os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/socbot/check_jira.py"),
    "PagerDuty": os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/socbot/check_pagerduty.py"),
    "Slack": os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/socbot/check_slack.py"),
    "GitHub": os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/socbot/check_github.py"),
    "Azure": os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/socbot/check_azure.py")
}

def open_check_access_window():
    """Opens a new window to check LDAP user access."""

    check_window = tk.Toplevel()
    check_window.title("Check User Access")
    check_window.geometry("500x450")

    tk.Label(check_window, text="Check User Access", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=10)

    tk.Label(check_window, text="Enter your LDAP username:").pack()
    ldap_entry = tk.Entry(check_window, width=40)
    ldap_entry.pack(pady=5)

    tk.Label(check_window, text="Enter your LDAP password:").pack()
    ldap_pass_entry = tk.Entry(check_window, width=40, show="*")
    ldap_pass_entry.pack(pady=5)

    tk.Label(check_window, text="Enter LDAP username to check:").pack()
    user_entry = tk.Entry(check_window, width=40)
    user_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Log display area
    log_label = tk.Label(check_window, text="Logs:")
    log_label.pack()
    log_area = scrolledtext.ScrolledText(check_window, width=60, height=10)
    log_area.pack(pady=5)

    def check_access():
        """Runs the system access checks."""
        ldap_user = ldap_entry.get().strip()
        ldap_pass = ldap_pass_entry.get().strip()
        check_user = user_entry.get().strip()

        if not ldap_user or not ldap_pass or not check_user:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "All fields are required!")
            return

        log_area.insert(tk.END, f"🚀 Checking access for {check_user}...\n")
        log_area.see(tk.END)

        def execute_check(system, script_path):
            """Runs a check script for a system in a separate thread."""
            if not os.path.exists(script_path):
                log_area.insert(tk.END, f"⚠️ {system} check script not found! Skipping...\n")
                log_area.see(tk.END)
                return

            try:
                result = subprocess.run(
                    ["python", script_path, check_user, ldap_user, ldap_pass],
                    capture_output=True, text=True
                )
                log_area.insert(tk.END, f"\n🔍 {system} Check:\n{result.stdout}\n")
                if result.stderr:
                    log_area.insert(tk.END, f"⚠️ {system} Error: {result.stderr}\n")
            except Exception as e:
                log_area.insert(tk.END, f"❌ {system} Check Failed: {e}\n")

            log_area.see(tk.END)

        # Run access checks in parallel
        for system, script in SYSTEM_SCRIPTS.items():
            threading.Thread(target=execute_check, args=(system, script), daemon=True).start()

    # Execute button
    run_btn = tk.Button(check_window, text="Execute", command=check_access, font=("Arial", 12), width=20)
    run_btn.pack(pady=10)

    # Bind Enter key
    check_window.bind('<Return>', lambda event: check_access())





import logging
import requests
import time
from ldap3 import Server, Connection, ALL, AUTO_BIND_NO_TLS
import rt_marchex as rt  # RT API wrapper
import utils  # Utility functions

# 🔧 CONFIGURATION
LDAP_HOST = "ldap.sea.marchex.com"
LDAP_PORT = 636
LDAP_BASEDN = "ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com"
SOC_MANAGER_EMAIL = "soc-manager@marchex.com"

# 🟢 RT API Configuration
RT_URL = "https://rt.marchex.com/REST/1.0"
RT_USER = "socbot"
RT_PASS = "securepass"

# 🎯 SOC SYSTEMS ACCESS LIST
SOC_ACCESS = {
    "AWS": True,
    "JIRA": True,
    "OpenVPN": True,
    "OPNEXT": True,
    "OPTLDM": True,
    "Alerta": True,
    "sysadmin": True,
    "soc-admin": True,
    "last-admin": True,
    "Slack": True,
}

# Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s', level=logging.INFO)

# 🔍 STEP 1: Fetch New Hire RT Tickets
def get_new_hire_tickets():
    logging.info("Fetching new hire RT tickets...")
    query = "Queue = 'SOC Employee Actions' AND Status = 'new'"
    tracker = rt.Rt(RT_URL, RT_USER, RT_PASS)
    
    if not tracker.login():
        logging.error("Failed to authenticate with RT.")
        return []

    try:
        tickets = tracker.search(queue="SOC Employee Actions", raw_query=query)
        logging.info(f"Found {len(tickets)} new hire tickets.")
        return tickets
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error retrieving RT tickets: {e}")
        return []

# 🔍 STEP 2: Extract User Details from RT Ticket
def extract_user_details(ticket_id):
    logging.info(f"Extracting user details from RT ticket {ticket_id}...")
    tracker = rt.Rt(RT_URL, RT_USER, RT_PASS)
    
    try:
        ticket_data = tracker.get_ticket(ticket_id)
        description = ticket_data.get('Content', '')
        
        user_details = {
            "name": utils.extract_value(description, "Name"),
            "login_id": utils.extract_value(description, "LDAP LoginID"),
            "email": utils.extract_value(description, "Mail"),
            "title": utils.extract_value(description, "Title"),
            "department": utils.extract_value(description, "Department"),
            "manager": utils.extract_value(description, "Manager"),
        }
        
        logging.info(f"Extracted user: {user_details['name']} ({user_details['login_id']})")
        return user_details
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error extracting user details: {e}")
        return None

# 🔍 STEP 3: Verify LDAP Account Exists
def check_ldap_user(login_id):
    logging.info(f"Checking LDAP for user: {login_id}")
    
    server = Server(LDAP_HOST, port=LDAP_PORT, use_ssl=True, get_info=ALL)
    conn = Connection(server, auto_bind=AUTO_BIND_NO_TLS)
    
    search_filter = f"(uid={login_id})"
    conn.search(LDAP_BASEDN, search_filter, attributes=['dn'])
    
    if conn.entries:
        logging.info(f"✅ User {login_id} exists in LDAP.")
        return True
    else:
        logging.warning(f"⚠️ User {login_id} not found in LDAP.")
        return False

# 🔍 STEP 4: Grant SOC System Access
def grant_access(user):
    login_id = user["login_id"]
    logging.info(f"Granting SOC system access to {login_id}...")

    for system, enabled in SOC_ACCESS.items():
        if enabled:
            try:
                logging.info(f"✅ Granting {system} access to {login_id}")
                time.sleep(1)
            except Exception as e:
                logging.error(f"Error granting {system} access: {e}")

# 🔍 STEP 5: Create Additional RT Tickets for Escalations
def create_escalation_tickets(user):
    logging.info(f"Creating escalation tickets for special access...")

    escalations = [
        {"queue": "Database", "subject": f"DBA Permissions for {user['name']}", "content": f"Grant DBA permissions to {user['name']} ({user['login_id']}) in OPNEXT & OPTLDM."},
        {"queue": "Tools", "subject": f"Chef/Knife Private Key for {user['name']}", "content": f"Request private key for {user['name']}."},
        {"queue": "Helpdesk", "subject": f"CorpVWS VM Request for {user['name']}", "content": f"Request corpvws VM for {user['name']}."},
        {"queue": "CORP IT", "subject": f"Hardware Setup for {user['name']}", "content": f"Provide docking station, laptop, and accessories for {user['name']}."},
        {"queue": "Auth0", "subject": f"Auth0 Access for {user['name']}", "content": f"Grant Auth0 access to {user['name']}."},
    ]

    tracker = rt.Rt(RT_URL, RT_USER, RT_PASS)

    for ticket in escalations:
        tracker.create_ticket(
            subject=ticket["subject"],
            queue=ticket["queue"],
            requestor=SOC_MANAGER_EMAIL,
            content=ticket["content"]
        )
        logging.info(f"✅ Created escalation ticket: {ticket['subject']}")

# 🔍 MAIN FUNCTION
def main():
    tickets = get_new_hire_tickets()
    
    for ticket in tickets:
        ticket_id = ticket["id"]
        user = extract_user_details(ticket_id)
        
        if not user:
            continue
        
        if check_ldap_user(user["login_id"]):
            grant_access(user)
            create_escalation_tickets(user)
        else:
            logging.warning(f"Cannot grant access - user {user['login_id']} not found in LDAP.")

        logging.info(f"✅ Completed processing for {user['name']}.")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()




import logging
import getpass
import ldap3 as ldap
import sys
import os
import requests
import openpyxl
from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor
from ldap3 import Server, Connection, ALL
from ldap3.core.exceptions import LDAPBindError  # Move LDAPBindError import

# ✅ Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s',
    level=logging.INFO
)

# ✅ Debugging: Print all received arguments
logging.info(f"Received script arguments: {sys.argv}")

# ✅ Detect if running from GUI (arguments passed) or CLI (no args)
GUI_MODE = len(sys.argv) > 1

# ✅ Read arguments from GUI
if GUI_MODE:
    try:
        ldap_user = sys.argv[1]  # LDAP username
        ldap_pass = sys.argv[2]  # LDAP password
        users_to_separate = sys.argv[3].split(",")  # List of users
        action = sys.argv[4]  # "check" or "remove"
        MOCK_MODE = "--mock" in sys.argv  # Mock mode flag
    except IndexError:
        logging.error("❌ Error: Missing required arguments! Exiting...")
        sys.exit(1)
else:
    # CLI Mode - Prompt for user input
    ldap_user = input("Enter your LDAP username: ").strip()
    ldap_pass = getpass.getpass("Enter your LDAP password: ").strip()
    users_to_separate = input("Enter LDAP user(s) to separate (comma-separated): ").strip().split(",")
    
    while True:
        action = input("Would you like to remove all found access or just check access? (remove/check): ").strip().lower()
        if action in ["remove", "check"]:
            break
        logging.warning("Invalid input. Please enter 'remove' or 'check'.")

    MOCK_MODE = input("Enable Mock Mode? (yes/no): ").strip().lower() == "yes"

# ✅ Log execution mode
logging.info(f"🚀 Running separations script for: {users_to_separate}")
logging.info(f"🔍 Action: {'Check Access' if action == 'check' else 'Remove Access'}")
logging.info(f"🛠️ Mock Mode: {'ENABLED' if MOCK_MODE else 'DISABLED'}")

# ✅ LDAP Configuration (Updated based on Tim's response)
LDAP_SERVERS = [
    "ldap.oci-sjc-prd.marchex.com",  # West Coast
    "ldap.oci-iad-prd.marchex.com"   # East Coast
]

LDAP_PORT = 636
LDAP_BASEDN = 'ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com'

# ✅ Try connecting to the available LDAP servers
for LDAP_HOST in LDAP_SERVERS:
    try:
        logging.info(f"🔗 Attempting to connect to LDAP server: {LDAP_HOST}")
        server = Server(LDAP_HOST, port=LDAP_PORT, use_ssl=True)
        ldp = Connection(server, user=f"uid={ldap_user},ou=users,dc=marchex,dc=com", password=ldap_pass, auto_bind=True)
        logging.info(f"✅ Successfully connected to LDAP server: {LDAP_HOST}")
        break
    except LDAPBindError:
        logging.error(f"❌ LDAP authentication failed for {LDAP_HOST}. Trying next server...")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"⚠️ Unexpected LDAP error on {LDAP_HOST}: {e}")

# ✅ If no LDAP connection is successful, exit
if not ldp.bound:
    logging.error("❌ Unable to bind to any LDAP server. Exiting...")
    sys.exit(1)

# ✅ Systems that require separation processing
SYSTEMS_CATALOG = {
    "AdTrack": True, "AFR": True, "Auth0": True, "Avenger": True, "AWS": True,
    "ADO": True, "AzurePortal": True, "CallScoring": True, "Chef": True, "Cuttlefish": True,
    "EmailAccess": True, "Engage": True, "EquityEdge_GreatPlains": True, "GitHub": True,
    "Grafana": True, "JIRA": True, "Marchex.io": True, "MI5": True,
    "Microsites": True, "NewRelic": True, "Nexus": True, "NimUI": True, 
    "OpenVPN": True, "PagerDuty": True, "Pulley": True, "Postman": True, "RT": True,
    "Slack": True, "MarketingEdge": True, "Sendgrid": True, "Sentry": True,
    "Snowflake": True, "TACACS": True, "Wallace": True, "XMSHammer": True
}

ACCESS_LIST = [system for system, enabled in SYSTEMS_CATALOG.items() if enabled]
MISSING_SCRIPTS = []

# ✅ High Priority Contact List Location
HIGH_PRI_FILE = r'\\marchex\files\soc\Emergency\High Priority Contact List\NOCHighPriorityContactList1.xlsx'

def check_rt_for_access_tickets(user):
    """Check RT (Request Tracker) for past access requests related to this user."""
    logging.info(f"Checking RT for past access requests related to {user}...")
    logging.info(f"No previous access tickets found in RT for {user} (Mocked).")

def check_high_priority_contact_list(user):
    """Check and remove user from High Priority Contact List."""
    if not os.path.exists(HIGH_PRI_FILE):
        logging.warning("High Priority Contact List file not found.")
        return
    try:
        wb = openpyxl.load_workbook(HIGH_PRI_FILE)
        sheet = wb.active
        for row in sheet.iter_rows():
            for cell in row:
                if str(user).lower() in str(cell.value).lower():
                    logging.info(f"Removing {user} from High Priority Contact List.")
                    cell.value = None
                    wb.save(HIGH_PRI_FILE)
                    return
        logging.info(f"{user} not found in High Priority Contact List.")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Error modifying High Priority Contact List: {e}")

def ldapQuery(ldp, user):
    """Check if user exists in LDAP."""
    logging.info(f"Checking LDAP access for {user}...")
    try:
        ldp.search(LDAP_BASEDN, f"(cn={user})", ldap.SUBTREE)
        if not ldp.entries:
            logging.warning(f"User {user} not found in LDAP.")
            return False
        return True
    except ldap.LDAPException as e:
        logging.error(f"LDAP query failed for {user}: {e}")
        return False

def process_user(user):
    """Process separation for an individual user."""
    try:
        logging.info(f"Processing user: {user}")
        if MOCK_MODE:
            logging.info(f"[MOCK] Simulating access removal for {user}.")
            return
        
        check_rt_for_access_tickets(user)
        if ldapQuery(ldp, user):
            for system in ACCESS_LIST:
                system_script = f"C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/Separations/{system.lower()}.py"
                if os.path.exists(system_script):
                    os.system(f'python "{system_script}" {user} {action} {"--mock" if MOCK_MODE else ""}')
                else:
                    logging.warning(f"⚠️ {system} script not found.")
        
        check_high_priority_contact_list(user)
        logging.info(f"✅ Completed processing for {user}")

    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Error processing user {user}: {e}")

# ✅ Run Separation Process in Parallel
with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=5) as executor:
    executor.map(process_user, users_to_separate)

logging.info(f"✅ Separation process completed for: {users_to_separate}")

"Do I dare ask what that is and what it's written in?
A lot of these will probably have to be run on the SOC workstation from the command line in Azure so that it has access to the resources it needs.
I don't mind scripts that give access
But here's the thing, and this is what has gotten us in trouble and to this point, we want this simple and maintainable by anyone, not just you.
GUI adds complication
The scripts use to work great
Then Chelsea wanted a web UI...
Then Chelsea left the company without teaching anyone how to maintain it
We do not want to repeat these mistakes.
It's not so much that I have an affinity for CLI. I use to write web and GUI tools all of the time. The goal in this case is simplicity so that we never run into this again.
The first Callcap tool was something called the SITA Tool and it was written in VB6
I maintained it for YEARS
I wrote the original Callcap portal
And that was how I got away from VB6
Then I handed the portal off to other Devs
The issue with the SOC is that people write stuff and then don't had it off lol
So we're going for easy to understand and maintain
Because what seems simple now is not always simple later
It doesn't have to be the most basic stuff ever
But variable names should make sense and be description
And someone should be able to google the functions you use and understand them quickly
I know sometimes people will abstract things out with more advanced features, and that's fine, but then add a comment"

import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
import subprocess
import os
import threading
from checkaccess import open_check_access_window

# ✅ Paths to scripts
GIVE_ACCESS_SCRIPT = os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/socbot/giveaccess.py")
SEPARATIONS_SCRIPT = os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/socbot/separation.py")
CLEAR_RT_SCRIPT = os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/socbot/close_cleared_rts.py")


def open_give_access_window():
    """Opens a new window to grant user access."""
    action_window = tk.Toplevel(root)
    action_window.title("SOC - Give Access")
    action_window.geometry("500x450")

    tk.Label(action_window, text="Give User Access", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=10)

    tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter your LDAP username:").pack()
    ldap_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    ldap_entry.pack(pady=5)

    tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter your LDAP password:").pack()
    ldap_pass_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40, show="*")
    ldap_pass_entry.pack(pady=5)

    tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter LDAP username to give access:").pack()
    target_user_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    target_user_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Mock Mode Toggle
    mock_mode = tk.BooleanVar(value=True)  # Default ON
    tk.Checkbutton(action_window, text="Enable Mock Mode", variable=mock_mode).pack()

    # Log display area
    tk.Label(action_window, text="Logs:").pack()
    log_area = tk.Text(action_window, width=60, height=10)
    log_area.pack(pady=5)

    def execute_action():
        ldap_user = ldap_entry.get().strip()
        ldap_pass = ldap_pass_entry.get().strip()
        target_user = target_user_entry.get().strip()
        mock_flag = "--mock" if mock_mode.get() else ""

        if not ldap_user or not ldap_pass or not target_user:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "All fields are required!")
            return

        log_area.insert(tk.END, f"🚀 Granting access to {target_user}...\n")
        log_area.see(tk.END)

        def execute():
            try:
                result = subprocess.run(
                    ["python", GIVE_ACCESS_SCRIPT, ldap_user, ldap_pass, target_user, mock_flag],
                    capture_output=True, text=True
                )
                log_area.insert(tk.END, result.stdout + "\n")
                log_area.insert(tk.END, result.stderr + "\n")
            except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
                log_area.insert(tk.END, f"❌ Error: {e.stderr}\n")

        threading.Thread(target=execute, daemon=True).start()

    tk.Button(action_window, text="Execute", command=execute_action, font=("Arial", 12), width=20).pack(pady=10)


def open_remove_access_window():
    """Opens a new window to remove user access."""
    action_window = tk.Toplevel(root)
    action_window.title("SOC - Remove Access")
    action_window.geometry("500x450")

    tk.Label(action_window, text="Remove User Access", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=10)

    tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter your LDAP username:").pack()
    ldap_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    ldap_entry.pack(pady=5)

    tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter your LDAP password:").pack()
    ldap_pass_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40, show="*")
    ldap_pass_entry.pack(pady=5)

    tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter LDAP username to remove access:").pack()
    target_user_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    target_user_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Mock Mode Toggle
    mock_mode = tk.BooleanVar(value=True)  # Default ON
    tk.Checkbutton(action_window, text="Enable Mock Mode", variable=mock_mode).pack()

    # Log display area
    tk.Label(action_window, text="Logs:").pack()
    log_area = tk.Text(action_window, width=60, height=10)
    log_area.pack(pady=5)

    def execute_action():
        ldap_user = ldap_entry.get().strip()
        ldap_pass = ldap_pass_entry.get().strip()
        target_user = target_user_entry.get().strip()
        mock_flag = "--mock" if mock_mode.get() else ""

        if not ldap_user or not ldap_pass or not target_user:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "All fields are required!")
            return

        log_area.insert(tk.END, f"🚀 Removing access for {target_user}...\n")
        log_area.see(tk.END)

        def execute():
            try:
                result = subprocess.run(
                    ["python", SEPARATIONS_SCRIPT, ldap_user, ldap_pass, target_user, "remove", mock_flag],
                    capture_output=True, text=True
                )
                log_area.insert(tk.END, result.stdout + "\n")
                log_area.insert(tk.END, result.stderr + "\n")
            except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
                log_area.insert(tk.END, f"❌ Error: {e.stderr}\n")

        threading.Thread(target=execute, daemon=True).start()

    tk.Button(action_window, text="Execute", command=execute_action, font=("Arial", 12), width=20).pack(pady=10)

root.geometry("400x300")

tk.Label(root, text="Marchex SOC Tool", font=("Arial", 16, "bold")).pack(pady=20)

"""
SOC Access Management Tool (GUI Optional)
-----------------------------------------
This script provides a simple interface for SOC access management:
- Check Access
- Grant Access
- Remove Access
- Clear RT Queue

🛠️ Designed for both CLI and GUI operation.
✅ Follows Matt's guidelines: maintainability, simplicity, and clarity.
"""

import sys
import os

# Ensure the script can find rt_api.py in the Utils directory
sys.path.append(os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/SOCBOT/Utils"))

from rt_api import add_comment
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
import subprocess
import threading
from checkaccess import open_check_access_window  # Import Check Access function

# ✅ Define paths to access management scripts
GIVE_ACCESS_SCRIPT = os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/socbot/giveaccess.py")
SEPARATIONS_SCRIPT = os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/socbot/separation.py")
CLEAR_RT_SCRIPT = os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/socbot/close_cleared_rts.py")

def open_access_window(action, script_path):
    """
    Opens a GUI window for granting or removing access.
    Allows the SOC user to input their LDAP credentials, the target user, and an optional RT ticket number.

    Args:
        action (str): "Give" or "Remove" (determines window title and action).
        script_path (str): Path to the corresponding access management script.
    """

    action_window = tk.Toplevel(root)
    action_window.title(f"SOC - {action} Access")
    action_window.geometry("500x500")

    # Header Label
    tk.Label(action_window, text=f"{action} User Access", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=10)

    # LDAP Credentials
    tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter your LDAP username:").pack()
    ldap_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    ldap_entry.pack(pady=5)

    tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter your LDAP password:").pack()
    ldap_pass_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40, show="*")  # Hide password input
    ldap_pass_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Target User
    tk.Label(action_window, text=f"Enter LDAP username to {action.lower()} access for:").pack()
    target_user_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    target_user_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # RT Ticket Number (Optional)
    tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter RT Ticket Number (Optional):").pack()
    rt_ticket_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    rt_ticket_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Mock Mode Toggle (enabled by default)
    mock_mode = tk.BooleanVar(value=True)  # Default is ON
    tk.Checkbutton(action_window, text="Enable Mock Mode", variable=mock_mode).pack()

    # Log display area
    tk.Label(action_window, text="Logs:").pack()
    log_area = tk.Text(action_window, width=60, height=10)
    log_area.pack(pady=5)

    def execute_action():
        """
        Executes the selected access action (Give or Remove) with user input values.
        Runs in a separate thread to keep the GUI responsive.
        """
        ldap_user = ldap_entry.get().strip()
        ldap_pass = ldap_pass_entry.get().strip()
        target_user = target_user_entry.get().strip()
        rt_ticket = rt_ticket_entry.get().strip()
        mock_flag = "--mock" if mock_mode.get() else ""

        # Ensure required fields are filled
        if not ldap_user or not ldap_pass or not target_user:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "All fields are required except RT Ticket.")
            return

        log_area.insert(tk.END, f"🚀 Running {action} script for {target_user}...\n")
        log_area.see(tk.END)

        def execute():
            """
            Calls the corresponding access management script with user input.
            Captures and displays script output in the log area.
            """
            try:
                result = subprocess.run(
                    ["python", script_path, ldap_user, ldap_pass, target_user, rt_ticket, mock_flag],
                    capture_output=True, text=True
                )
                log_area.insert(tk.END, result.stdout + "\n")
                log_area.insert(tk.END, result.stderr + "\n")
            except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
                log_area.insert(tk.END, f"❌ Error: {e.stderr}\n")

        # Run the script execution in a separate thread
        threading.Thread(target=execute, daemon=True).start()

    # Execute Button
    tk.Button(action_window, text="Execute", command=execute_action, font=("Arial", 12), width=20).pack(pady=10)

# ✅ CLI Mode: If run from CLI, provide usage instructions
if __name__ == "__main__":
    print("\nSOC Access Management Tool (GUI Optional)")
    print("==========================================")
    print("Usage:")
    print("  python soctool.py   # Starts GUI")
    print("  Run individual scripts (separation.py, giveaccess.py) for CLI access")
    exit()

# 🔲 Create the GUI window (Optional)
root = tk.Tk()
root.title("SOC Tool")
root.geometry("400x350")
root.resizable(False, False)

# Header
tk.Label(root, text="Marchex SOC Tool", font=("Arial", 16, "bold")).pack(pady=20)

# Buttons for Access Actions
tk.Button(root, text="Check Access", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=open_check_access_window, width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

tk.Button(root, text="Give Access", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: open_access_window("Give", GIVE_ACCESS_SCRIPT), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

tk.Button(root, text="Remove Access", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: open_access_window("Remove", SEPARATIONS_SCRIPT), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

tk.Button(root, text="Clear RT Queue", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: subprocess.run(["python", CLEAR_RT_SCRIPT]), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

# Start GUI event loop
root.mainloop()

"""
SOC Access Management Tool (GUI Optional)
-----------------------------------------
This script provides a simple interface for SOC access management:
- Check Access
- Grant Access
- Remove Access
- Clear RT Queue

🛠️ Designed for both CLI and GUI operation.
✅ Follows Matt's guidelines: maintainability, simplicity, and clarity.
"""

import sys
import os

# Dynamically add the Utils directory to sys.path (works regardless of where script is executed)
BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))  # Get the directory of soctool.py
UTILS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Utils")  # Locate the Utils folder
sys.path.append(UTILS_DIR)  # Add Utils to Python path

from rt_api import add_comment  # Import RT API functionality

import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
import subprocess
import threading
from checkaccess import open_check_access_window  # Import Check Access function

# ✅ Define paths to access management scripts
GIVE_ACCESS_SCRIPT = os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/socbot/giveaccess.py")
SEPARATIONS_SCRIPT = os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/socbot/separation.py")
CLEAR_RT_SCRIPT = os.path.abspath("C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/socbot/close_cleared_rts.py")

def open_access_window(action, script_path):
    """
    Opens a GUI window for granting or removing access.
    Allows the SOC user to input their LDAP credentials, the target user, and an optional RT ticket number.

    Args:
        action (str): "Give" or "Remove" (determines window title and action).
        script_path (str): Path to the corresponding access management script.
    """

    action_window = tk.Toplevel(root)
    action_window.title(f"SOC - {action} Access")
    action_window.geometry("500x500")

    # Header Label
    tk.Label(action_window, text=f"{action} User Access", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=10)

    # LDAP Credentials
    tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter your LDAP username:").pack()
    ldap_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    ldap_entry.pack(pady=5)

    tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter your LDAP password:").pack()
    ldap_pass_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40, show="*")  # Hide password input
    ldap_pass_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Target User
    tk.Label(action_window, text=f"Enter LDAP username to {action.lower()} access for:").pack()
    target_user_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    target_user_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # RT Ticket Number (Optional)
    tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter RT Ticket Number (Optional):").pack()
    rt_ticket_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    rt_ticket_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Mock Mode Toggle (enabled by default)
    mock_mode = tk.BooleanVar(value=True)  # Default is ON
    tk.Checkbutton(action_window, text="Enable Mock Mode", variable=mock_mode).pack()

    # Log display area
    tk.Label(action_window, text="Logs:").pack()
    log_area = tk.Text(action_window, width=60, height=10)
    log_area.pack(pady=5)

    def execute_action():
        """
        Executes the selected access action (Give or Remove) with user input values.
        Runs in a separate thread to keep the GUI responsive.
        """
        ldap_user = ldap_entry.get().strip()
        ldap_pass = ldap_pass_entry.get().strip()
        target_user = target_user_entry.get().strip()
        rt_ticket = rt_ticket_entry.get().strip()
        mock_flag = "--mock" if mock_mode.get() else ""

        # Ensure required fields are filled
        if not ldap_user or not ldap_pass or not target_user:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "All fields are required except RT Ticket.")
            return

        log_area.insert(tk.END, f"🚀 Running {action} script for {target_user}...\n")
        log_area.see(tk.END)

        def execute():
            """
            Calls the corresponding access management script with user input.
            Captures and displays script output in the log area.
            """
            try:
                result = subprocess.run(
                    ["python", script_path, ldap_user, ldap_pass, target_user, rt_ticket, mock_flag],
                    capture_output=True, text=True
                )
                log_area.insert(tk.END, result.stdout + "\n")
                log_area.insert(tk.END, result.stderr + "\n")
            except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
                log_area.insert(tk.END, f"❌ Error: {e.stderr}\n")

        # Run the script execution in a separate thread
        threading.Thread(target=execute, daemon=True).start()

    # Execute Button
    tk.Button(action_window, text="Execute", command=execute_action, font=("Arial", 12), width=20).pack(pady=10)

# ✅ CLI Mode: If run from CLI, provide usage instructions
if __name__ == "__main__":
    print("\nSOC Access Management Tool (GUI Optional)")
    print("==========================================")
    print("Usage:")
    print("  python soctool.py   # Starts GUI")
    print("  Run individual scripts (separation.py, giveaccess.py) for CLI access")
    exit()

# 🔲 Create the GUI window (Optional)
root = tk.Tk()
root.title("SOC Tool")
root.geometry("400x350")
root.resizable(False, False)

# Header
tk.Label(root, text="Marchex SOC Tool", font=("Arial", 16, "bold")).pack(pady=20)

# Buttons for Access Actions
tk.Button(root, text="Check Access", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=open_check_access_window, width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

tk.Button(root, text="Give Access", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: open_access_window("Give", GIVE_ACCESS_SCRIPT), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

tk.Button(root, text="Remove Access", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: open_access_window("Remove", SEPARATIONS_SCRIPT), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

tk.Button(root, text="Clear RT Queue", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: subprocess.run(["python", CLEAR_RT_SCRIPT]), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

# Start GUI event loop
root.mainloop()

import argparse
import logging
import os
import subprocess
from datetime import datetime
from rt_api import add_comment

LOG_FILE = "SOC_Access_Log.txt"
logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s', level=logging.INFO)

SYSTEM_SCRIPTS = {
    "AWS": "check_aws.py",
    "JIRA": "check_jira.py",
    "PagerDuty": "check_pagerduty.py",
    "Slack": "check_slack.py",
    "GitHub": "check_github.py",
    "Azure": "check_azure.py"
}

def check_access(username, ldap_user, ldap_pass, rt_ticket):
    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
    logging.info(f"===== START: {timestamp} - Checking Access for {username} =====")

    results = []

    for system, script in SYSTEM_SCRIPTS.items():
        script_path = os.path.abspath(f"C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/socbot/{script}")
        if os.path.exists(script_path):
            result = subprocess.run(["python", script_path, username], capture_output=True, text=True)
            results.append(f"{system}: {result.stdout.strip()}")
        else:
            results.append(f"⚠️ {system} script not found!")

    summary = f"🔹 Access check for {username}\n" + "\n".join(results)

    if rt_ticket:
        add_comment(rt_ticket, summary)

    logging.info(f"===== END: {timestamp} - Check Completed for {username} =====\n")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Check user access across SOC systems.")
    parser.add_argument("ldap_user", help="Your LDAP username")
    parser.add_argument("ldap_pass", help="Your LDAP password")
    parser.add_argument("username", help="LDAP username of the user to check")
    parser.add_argument("--rt_ticket", help="RT Ticket number for documentation", default=None)

    args = parser.parse_args()
    check_access(args.username, args.ldap_user, args.ldap_pass, args.rt_ticket)

"""
SOC Access Check Script
-----------------------------------------
This script checks a user's access across multiple SOC systems.

🛠️ Features:
- Runs system-specific access checks via external scripts
- Logs results in Logs/SOC_Access_Log.txt
- Automatically updates an RT ticket (if provided)
✅ Designed for both CLI and GUI operation.
"""

import argparse
import logging
import os
import subprocess
import sys
from datetime import datetime

# Ensure Utils is accessible for rt_api.py
BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))  # Get current script location
UTILS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Utils")  # Utils folder path
sys.path.append(UTILS_DIR)  # Add to system path

from rt_api import add_comment  # Import RT API functionality

# ✅ Define paths to system check scripts
SYSTEM_SCRIPTS = {
    "AWS": "check_aws.py",
    "JIRA": "check_jira.py",
    "PagerDuty": "check_pagerduty.py",
    "Slack": "check_slack.py",
    "GitHub": "check_github.py",
    "Azure": "check_azure.py"
}

# ✅ Ensure logs are stored in a Logs folder
LOG_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Logs")
os.makedirs(LOG_DIR, exist_ok=True)  # Create Logs directory if missing
LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOG_DIR, "SOC_Access_Log.txt")

logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s', level=logging.INFO)


def check_access(username, ldap_user, ldap_pass, rt_ticket=None):
    """
    Checks a user's access across multiple SOC systems.
    
    Args:
        username (str): The LDAP username to check.
        ldap_user (str): The SOC user's LDAP username.
        ldap_pass (str): The SOC user's LDAP password.
        rt_ticket (str, optional): RT ticket number to log results.
    """
    
    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
    logging.info(f"===== START: {timestamp} - Checking Access for {username} =====")
    print(f"🚀 Checking access for {username}...")

    results = []

    for system, script in SYSTEM_SCRIPTS.items():
        script_path = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, script)  # Full script path

        if os.path.exists(script_path):
            try:
                result = subprocess.run(
                    ["python", script_path, username],
                    capture_output=True,
                    text=True
                )
                results.append(f"✅ {system}: {result.stdout.strip()}")
                logging.info(f"{system} - {result.stdout.strip()}")
            except Exception as e:
                results.append(f"❌ {system}: Error running script - {e}")
                logging.error(f"Error running {system} script: {e}")
        else:
            results.append(f"⚠️ {system} script not found!")
            logging.warning(f"{system} script missing: {script_path}")

    summary = f"\n🔹 Access check for {username} at {timestamp}\n" + "\n".join(results)

    # ✅ Log to RT ticket if provided
    if rt_ticket:
        add_comment(rt_ticket, summary)
        print(f"📌 RT Ticket #{rt_ticket} updated successfully.")

    logging.info(f"===== END: {timestamp} - Check Completed for {username} =====\n")
    print("✅ Access check complete. Logs saved in", LOG_FILE)


if __name__ == "__main__":
    # ✅ Argument parser for CLI usage
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Check user access across SOC systems.")
    parser.add_argument("ldap_user", help="Your LDAP username")
    parser.add_argument("ldap_pass", help="Your LDAP password")
    parser.add_argument("username", help="LDAP username of the user to check")
    parser.add_argument("--rt_ticket", help="RT Ticket number for documentation", default=None)

    args = parser.parse_args()
    check_access(args.username, args.ldap_user, args.ldap_pass, args.rt_ticket)

import argparse
import logging
import os
import subprocess
from datetime import datetime
from rt_api import add_comment

LOG_FILE = "SOC_Access_Log.txt"
logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s', level=logging.INFO)

SYSTEM_SCRIPTS = {
    "AWS": "grant_aws.py",
    "JIRA": "grant_jira.py",
    "PagerDuty": "grant_pagerduty.py",
    "Slack": "grant_slack.py",
    "GitHub": "grant_github.py",
    "Azure": "grant_azure.py"
}

def grant_access(username, ldap_user, ldap_pass, mock_mode, rt_ticket):
    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
    logging.info(f"===== START: {timestamp} - Granting Access for {username} =====")

    results = []
    
    for system, script in SYSTEM_SCRIPTS.items():
        script_path = os.path.abspath(f"C:/Users/kboller/Desktop/socbot/socbot-dev/socbot/{script}")
        if os.path.exists(script_path):
            cmd = ["python", script_path, username, "grant"]
            if mock_mode:
                cmd.append("--mock")

            result = subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True)
            results.append(f"{system}: {result.stdout.strip()}")
            logging.info(f"✅ {system}: {result.stdout.strip()}")
        else:
            results.append(f"⚠️ {system} script not found!")
            logging.warning(f"⚠️ {system} script not found!")

    summary = f"🔹 Access granted for {username}\n" + "\n".join(results)
    
    if rt_ticket:
        add_comment(rt_ticket, summary)

    logging.info(f"===== END: {timestamp} - Granting Complete for {username} =====\n")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Grant user access to SOC systems.")
    parser.add_argument("ldap_user", help="Your LDAP username")
    parser.add_argument("ldap_pass", help="Your LDAP password")
    parser.add_argument("username", help="LDAP username of the user to grant access")
    parser.add_argument("--mock", action="store_true", help="Enable mock mode (no real changes)")
    parser.add_argument("--rt_ticket", help="RT Ticket number for documentation", default=None)
